International Telegrams Two

Japanese Privy Council Meeting Passes London Naval Treaty

Cabinet Meeting Today to Decide on Approval Procedures

(Dentsu, Tokyo, 1st) The plenary session of the Privy Council to conclude the approval of the London Naval Treaty was held in the palace at 10:00 this morning. On the Privy Council side, Vice-Presidents Kuratomi and Hiranuma, and Advisors Ito, Kaneko, and Kubota, etc., a total of 20 people, and secretaries and other officials below the rank of Second Secretary attended. On the government side, except for Minister of Communications Koizumi, who was absent due to illness, all cabinet members attended. At the appointed time, the Emperor arrived. The chairman announced the opening of the meeting. First, Ito, chairman of the review committee, reported on the committee's progress and its resolutions. Then, Prime Minister Hamaguchi explained the government's views and policies on the treaty. Then, questions were asked, but the main questions had already been completed by the review committee, and this was also a meeting before the Emperor, so no waves were stirred up. The naval treaty case was unanimously passed. After the meeting adjourned, Chairman Kuratomi immediately reported the resolution to the Emperor. The resolution will be handed over to the government on the same day. Starting at 10:00 AM on the morning of the 2nd, a temporary cabinet meeting will be held at the Prime Minister's residence, where Prime Minister Hamaguchi and other cabinet ministers will sign, and then the procedure for requesting approval will be taken.

New Austrian Cabinet Formed

Vogoin Appointed Prime Minister and Minister of National Defense

No Majority in Parliament

General Election in November

(Reuters, Vienna, 30th) The new Austrian cabinet has now been formed. Vogoin has been appointed Prime Minister and Minister of National Defense, and Seipel has been appointed Foreign Minister. However, the new cabinet cannot command a majority of deputies in parliament because the Greater German Party and the Farmers' Party refuse to join the government. The Federal Parliament will be dissolved immediately, and new elections will be held in November.

Mexico Forbids Chinese Immigrants from Entering

Announcing New Immigration Laws

Mexico City dispatch: The Mexican government has now announced a new immigration law, with four key points of amendment: (1) Preventing undesirable foreign immigrants from entering the country; (2) Establishing a consultative body composed of officials from relevant government departments; (3) Classifying foreign immigrants into the following three categories: (A) those who meet all requirements; (B) travelers; (C) immigrants with conditions; (4) Abolishing restrictions on those without special skills. After the Mexican government announced this immigration law, it immediately prohibited Chinese people from entering Mexico and decided to send back a portion of them. It has already ordered the Mexican ocean liner "Jiu" to depart from Manzanillo on the 22nd, carrying 55 Chinese people back to [Hong Kong]. (Hong Kong World)

Major Clash Between Cuban Students and Police

Shouting Slogans to Overthrow the President

Six People Seriously Wounded in Gunfire from Both Sides

Reuters dispatch, Havana, 30th: Cuban students and police clashed violently outside the Presidential Palace today. A group of students attempted to enter the Presidential Palace, firing shots into the air and shouting slogans to overthrow President Machado. Police rushed to block the students and attempted to disarm them. A burst of gunfire erupted, seriously wounding six people. The disturbance lasted for half an hour. In recent months, public sentiment has been quite agitated. Opponents of President Machado claim that the president is merely a puppet controlled by powerful American capitalists.

Japanese Naval Grand Maneuvers

To Be Held on the 26th of This Month

Rapid Advancements Since the Meiji Era

United Press dispatch, Tokyo, 1st: This year's special naval grand maneuvers will be held on October 26th in Kobe Harbor, with the Grand Fleet Review to be overseen by His Imperial Majesty the Emperor. A total of 165 warships will participate, with a total tonnage of 703,295 tons, along with 72 aircraft. The history of Japanese fleet reviews is as follows: The first was during the Meiji era, with 6 warships participating, totaling 2,453 tons. In Meiji 23, there were 19 ships, totaling 32,328 tons. In Meiji 38, there were 166 ships, totaling 325,559 tons. This year marks the 15th review, and the tonnage has increased more than 300 times compared to the first.

Three Russian Warships to Cruise the Mediterranean

Pacific dispatch, Riga, 30th: A Russian fleet, including one cruiser and two torpedo boats, will cruise the Mediterranean and refuel on the coasts of Constantinople, Greece, and Italy.

Soviet Reply to Finnish Note

An Extremely Strong Stance

Pacific dispatch, Moscow, 30th: People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs Litvinov recently replied to the Finnish envoy's note of September 16th, stating that the Finnish government had expelled its citizens from Soviet Russia. The Soviet government had raised a protest on July 16th. The note of September 16th stated that the expulsion of citizens was due to the "received country" movement, and that they were expelled towards the Soviet Russian border due to the contiguity of the two countries. Such language, regarding the violation of the Soviet Russian border, is intended to justify the invasion of Soviet Russia. If Finland allows the expelled people to return to their country, Soviet Russia will not obstruct it; otherwise, the Soviet government will consider Finland to have no intention of maintaining neighborly relations. This matter is a scene from the Lapua anti-[Communist] movement, and the Soviet attitude is quite strong.

Invention of a New Type of Anti-Aircraft Gun

A Powerful Tool for Aerial Defense

Pacific dispatch, Paris, September 10th: Recently in England, a new type of anti-aircraft gun has been invented, which can be placed in a fixed location or moved. The gun barrel has multiple grids, the width of which has never been seen before. The number of shots fired is greatly increased as a result. This gun has been tested by the Admiralty and is extremely satisfactory, and will soon be adopted on warships for aerial defense.

Domestic News

Northeastern Army Advances Towards the Pinghan and Pingsui Lines

Investigation of the Organization and Strength of the First Army

Beiping correspondence: The first batch of the Northeastern Army to move towards Pingjin (Beiping and Tianjin), Yu Xuezhong's First Army, completed mobilization by the night of the 25th. Wang Shuchang's Second Army began arriving in Tianjin on the 26th. It is said that these so-called First and Second Armies are not fixed designations, but rather are formed according to wartime corps organization. The First Army is composed of four infantry brigades, with an attached cavalry regiment and other configurations of engineer, transport, signal, and aviation units, roughly following the example of a Japanese wartime division. The Second Army is composed of three infantry brigades, plus one artillery regiment, with other engineer, transport, signal, and aviation units also like the First Army. There is also a Third Army, with Hu Yukun designated as the army commander. The unit has a prepared organization, but whether or not it will actually mobilize depends on the situation. If it is not urgently needed, mobilization will be halted, because Zhang Xueliang has adopted the military strategy decided by the Northeast Supreme Military Council, which is, as a first step, to have the First Army responsible for Beiping and its surroundings, and the Second Army responsible for Tianjin, the northern section of the Jinpu Railway, and a section of the Jinwan Railway. If there is a need to actively advance towards Baoding and other places along the Pinghan Railway, or if there is a possibility of war, then the second step would be to order the Third Army to move out, at which time the First Army would be moved to the Pinghan Railway. As far as the current situation is concerned, this is not yet under consideration, so whether Hu Yukun's Third Army will actually be organized and sent out is currently undecided. However, even considering only the First and Second Armies, their strength is already considerable. It is found that Yu's First Army's four brigades are actually equivalent to four formal divisions (the Northeastern Army abolished the division system after entering the Northeast in the 16th year of the Republic [1927], with the brigade being the highest peacetime unit; after the war against Russia last year, it was planned to restore the division system, but the reorganization costs were not finalized). Each brigade has an actual strength of between 10,000 and 11,700 men, and many were reorganized from previous armies or divisions. For example, the current Sixth Brigade of the First Army, under Li Zhentang, was formed by downsizing the former Eighth Army led by Wan Fulin. After Yu Xuezhong arrived in Beiping on the 26th, he held a military meeting with the four brigade commanders under his command at the headquarters in Tieshizi Hutong (the original site of Yan Xishan's Pingjin Garrison Headquarters) to properly allocate the stationing of the four brigades. (1) The entire 23rd Brigade (the old brigade commander was Ma Tingfu), which Yu concurrently commands, consisting of three regiments and six independent companies, will have one regiment stationed in the Temple of Heaven within Beiping city, and the six independent companies stationed at the old Navy Department (next door to the Garrison Headquarters). The other two regiments, one in Tianjin and one in Tangshan, are now being ordered to move entirely to the Pingjin Railway because Wang Shuchang's Second Army has already begun moving. (2) The entire 27th Brigade of Liu Naichang will be distributed from Fengtai Railway Station as a starting point, at key points along the Pinghan Railway such as Fengtai, Lugouqiao, Changxindian, Liangxiang, and Liulihe, taking a posture of waiting for orders to advance. (3) The entire Sixth Brigade of Li Zhentang will be distributed from the Xiyuan in the northwestern suburbs of Beiping, along the Pingsui Railway, at Qinghe, Shahe, Changping, and other places, all the way to Nankou. (4) The entire Fifth Brigade of Dong Yingbin will be stationed entirely within Beiping city and the Tongzhou area in the eastern suburbs. The above is the overall deployment of Yu's army. Analytically speaking, the task of Liu Naichang's and Li Zhentang's brigades is one for the Pinghan Railway and one for the Pingsui Railway, while the brigades of Dong Yingbin and Yu Xuezhong are concentrated in Beiping and are temporarily responsible for security. At the moment, general attention is being paid to the advancing actions of Liu's and Li's brigades, because the Jin army, which has retreated from various places west of Zhuozhou on the Pinghan Railway and north of Nankou on the Pingsui Railway, is gathering, and there seems to be no sign of continuing to yield defense. If the Northeastern Army's Liu and Li units actively advance, no one knows whether conflicts will arise. Yu Xuezhong issued a declaration yesterday upon arriving in Beiping, stating that if the other side peacefully yields, they will definitely not force it, so it is not possible to predict whether there will be any conflicts in the short term. Furthermore, according to the explanation of a certain Northeastern Army officer, the First Army's Liu and Li brigades being dispatched to Changxindian, Shahe, and other places along the Pinghan and Pingsui lines cannot be simply regarded as military actions of advancing towards the two lines, because those places are adjacent to Beiping and are defensive deployments that are essential for those guarding Beiping. (27th)

After the Northeastern Army Arrived in Tianjin

Tianjin correspondence: The Fifth Brigade, Sixth Brigade, Twenty-Third Brigade, Twenty-Seventh Brigade, and Second Cavalry Brigade of the Northeastern Army under Yu Xuezhong had completely arrived in the Pingjin area by noon on the 25th. Yesterday (the 24th), the security of this city was officially taken over by the Tenth Regiment of the Twenty-Third Brigade, under Li Choushan. Although there are still two remaining battalions of Jin army military police who have not left, they have already transported their weapons onto trains and will leave Tianjin for Shijiazhuang this afternoon. Yesterday morning, I went to the Beining Railway Bureau to visit Jiang Chunyan, Yu Xuezhong's representative. Jiang said that the defense of Beiping has been equipped and prepared. The Fifth Brigade and Sixth Brigade are responsible for the defense of the inner and outer cities of Beiping. The Twenty-Seventh Brigade is stationed in Fengtai and Changxindian. The Second Cavalry Brigade is stationed in Changping. The Twenty-Third Brigade is also stationed in Beiping, but the Tenth Regiment will remain temporarily responsible for the defense of Tianjin. After Wang Shuchang's Second Army arrives in Tianjin, the Tenth Regiment will leave for Beiping. While Mr. Jiang was talking, he was reading various telegrams, appearing very busy.

Since the arrival of the Northeastern Army in Tianjin, changes in personnel in various agencies are naturally to be expected. Lu Jinli, who concurrently served as the Acting Customs Commissioner, was eager to unload his responsibilities. On the 22nd, he was replaced by the original Customs Commissioner, Bi Luo. Zhang Yi, the director of the Jilu District Wheat Flour Special Tax Bureau, had already left his post. Chen Cengliang, the deputy director, was also not responsible. Former Secretary Shao Mingsheng received a telegram from Shanghai from Sun Qun, the former director, saying that he had received instructions from the Ministry of Finance to return to his post immediately. Shao then went to take over at 3:00 PM on the 23rd, and Chen handled the handover. In addition, the former Director of the Telephone Bureau, Chen Tirong, and the former Director of the Telegraph Bureau, Duanmu Bangfan, have not been able to fulfill their wishes because the current directors are unwilling to hand over.

The Hebei and Shanxi banks both experienced runs on the 21st. The Shanxi Bank announced its closure the next day (the 22nd). All the large and small banknotes circulating on the market, amounting to more than 150,000 yuan, were originally entrusted to the Zhongjiao and other banks for redemption and collection. Zhongjiao did not agree. The General Chamber of Commerce is currently handling the registration of the bank's banknotes. If it does not exceed 150,000 yuan, Zhongjiao and other banks may be able to redeem them. As for the Hebei Bank, since the day of the run, it has been redeeming without restrictions. Today is the fourth day, and there are not many banknotes circulating on the market. Its credit is actually better. A run also occurred at the Quan'ye Bank on the 23rd. It has now announced a one-week suspension of redemption, pending the arrival of funds from Shanghai, after which it will redeem. A run also occurred at the Agricultural and Industrial Bank on the 24th. Fortunately, it received strong assistance from the Zhongjiao and other banks, and it is hoped that it will subside. Liu Naichang, brigade commander of the Twenty-Seventh Brigade of the Da Zhongken Northeastern First Army.

The banknotes of the Yeliang banks were rejected by the market yesterday, and runs also occurred today. Recalling the changes in the situation in the past, turmoil is bound to occur in the financial world. The runs on various banks this time are also a phenomenon that should be expected. (Morning of September 25th)

A Record of Inspecting the Lub North Battlefield

From Jinan to Sangyuan

Jinan message: The Luokou Yellow River Railway Bridge. Before the Hebei Jin army retreated, Han Fuqu ordered Wei Jinglu, the leader of the Second Squad of the First Battalion of the Railway Team of the Second Transportation Corps, to be responsible for planning the repairs. After receiving the order, Leader Wei sent a car to Pukou to transport the originally unloaded materials and dispatched workers with the engineer Hu Shenghong of the Jinpu Railway. The Jin army withdrew on the 23rd. Leader Wei and Engineer Hu immediately went to supervise the repairs. The original intention was that it would take ten days to complete the project. Fortunately, the materials were available, and the General Headquarters telegraphed the Jiaoji Railway to borrow a crane, so construction began on the 25th and was completed early on the 27th. After the Luokou Bridge was repaired, Leader Wei and Engineer Hu prepared a special train early on the 27th, with thirteen material cars loaded with road repair materials, and took a team of more than one hundred engineers, departing from Jinan Station at 10:00 AM. (Since the Jin army withdrew from Jinan on August 15th, this is the first time a train has passed north of Jinan in more than forty days.) In addition to Wei and Hu, those traveling with the train included Li Yuhui, deputy to the Second Squad; Zhang Yuanhe, the head of the Jinan Locomotive Depot; (inspecting the route) Section Chief He of the General Affairs Office of the Pukou Railway Administration; Mao Qihuan, head of the Jinan Traffic Department (Mao was ordered by the Ministry of Railways to go to Tianjin to take over the Railway Administration, which was the original office, and Engineer Hu was also ordered to go with him. It is said that the deputy director of the Railway, Zhu Shuyun, has gone to Tianjin by sea to be responsible for the takeover). In order to understand the situation in Lub North, I discussed it with the railway team and received their consent to go north with the train. When the train arrived at Luokou, the Beiping armored train was on the bridge. After the Beiping train reversed, the special train went onto the bridge at 11:30 AM and slowly tested the train, arriving at the northern end of the bridge at 11:50 AM. (According to the regulations on the bridge, the speed must not exceed five miles per hour.) The crane was pulled back to the southern end, and after changing to a special train, it did not start until 1:30 PM. It arrived at Sangzidian at 2:00 PM and stopped slightly, arriving at Yancheng at 2:30 PM without stopping, and arriving at Yucheng at 3:30 PM, stopping to take on water. I got off the train to inspect and saw trenches densely distributed on both sides of the Tuhai River (according to the battle traces of the Han army guarding Yucheng), with new graves piled up, and countless civilian houses destroyed nearby. Among the losses along the way, this place suffered the most. The train departed at 4:00 PM, arriving at Zhangzhuang at 4:30 PM for a brief stop, and arriving at Pingyuan at 5:00 PM to stop. Sun Tongxuan, commander of the Twelfth Army, and Li Hanzhang, commander of the Eighty-Fifth Brigade, happened to be at the station. I presented my card to visit. Brigade Commander Li said that his brigade arrived in Shanghe on the 25th, and it was reported that a large part of Gao Guizi was in Leling. Because this brigade was ordered to concentrate in Pingyuan, it was inconvenient to divide the team to pursue. On the 26th, they passed Linzi and happened to encounter another unit of Gao's rebels, which they immediately surrounded, capturing more than two hundred people and seizing their weapons. They arrived in Pingyuan on the 27th, and this brigade was stationed in Pingyuan, waiting for further orders. Tang Yaoxun's unit of the Sixty-Fifth Brigade of the Twenty-Second Division was ordered to pursue Gao Guizi's unit and has now advanced to Wuding. Division Commander Gu (Liangmin) of the Twenty-Second Division led Ning Chunxiao's unit of the Sixty-Sixth Brigade and has arrived at the Yellow River Cliff, from where they will transfer to Dezhou. Army Commander Sun said that his unit arrived in Pingyuan on the 26th, and the army headquarters was located in the city. The directly subordinate units included an artillery regiment, a mortar regiment, and a company each of engineers, cavalry, and pistols. In addition, the entire Eighty-Fifth Brigade was ordered not to go to Dezhou temporarily. The unit in Yucheng was Ma Jingong's unit of the Sixtieth Brigade of this division. The Third Regiment was stationed in Yucheng, and the First Regiment was stationed in Yancheng. Zhao Xinde's unit of the Fifty-Ninth Banner of this division arrived in Dezhou on the 26th. It is rumored that the Northeastern Army has arrived in Lianzhen, but no report has been received yet. That place (Pingyuan) has not experienced war and has not suffered any losses. The special train departed at 5:00 PM, passing the old Yellow River and seeing the new trenches dug by the Jin army on both sides of the Majia River. Arriving in Dezhou at 6:30 PM, it was already dark, and the stationed troops were heavily guarded, so it was not convenient to get off the train and stayed on the train. It is estimated that there was no damage to any station or bridge along the way from Luokou to Dezhou, which was something we did not expect. The next morning (the 28th) at 8:10 AM, the engineering team attached Zhu Yupu took the original locomotive, attached one car, to Sangyuan to investigate. I also went along. Arriving in Sangyuan at 9:00 AM, that place is the border between Shandong and Hebei and is not stationed by any troops. There, I heard from the railway personnel that on the afternoon of the 27th, eight trains of the Northeastern Army arrived in Dongguang, and a small part arrived in Wuqiao County. Lianzhen and Anlingzhen will also send teams to station (but they have not arrived today). At 9:15 AM, we drove back from Sangyuan, arriving in Dezhou in thirty minutes. After I got off the train, I went to visit the stationed Brigade Commander Zhao. Zhao said that this brigade was the vanguard in this pursuit of the Jin army. At 2:30 PM on the 26th, they arrived in Dezhou from Pingyuan. Beforehand, they were ordered to resolve Qin Jianbin's new Second Division of recruits under Xie Zhendong, and they immediately took a company of men to the arsenal, disarming more than two hundred new recruits. More than one hundred people were also disarmed in Nanguan. All the prisoners who were willing to continue serving as soldiers have been selected and reorganized, and the rest have been sent back to their hometowns. The officers were all sent back to their original residences. Those stationed in Dezhou in this brigade include Zhang Tingyan's unit of the Second Regiment, Wu Yuanxing's unit of the Third Regiment, and the pistol team leader Zhang Yaode's unit. In addition, there are independent companies of engineers, mortars, and machine guns. Zhao Xiangxian's unit of the First Regiment is still in Jinan and will still be sent to the front in the coming days. In this battle, more than two thousand artillery shells and eight or nine carts were obtained in Pingyuan, capturing more than ten people. In Dezhou, forty boxes of bombs and mortar shells, one machine gun, more than ten assault machine guns, and more than one hundred rifles were obtained. This brigade was ordered to be stationed in Dezhou temporarily. Now Zhang Tiansheng, the new director of the Dezhou Public Security Bureau, has arrived, and Sun Tongfeng, the new county magistrate, has been additionally appointed. (It is said that Sun Tongxuan recommended him.

Page 8

He will arrive in Dezhou today.) Today, the special train from Jinan to Dezhou has arrived, and the county magistrates and public security directors along the route have all arrived with the train. It is heard that three trains of the Northeastern Army have arrived in Dongguang. The railway team's special train was ordered by Commander-in-Chief Han not to leave the Shandong border, so it departed from Dezhou at 0:20 PM today, stopping briefly in Pingyuan at 1:10 PM, not stopping in Zhangzhuang at 2:10 PM, and arriving in Yancheng at 3:30 PM, when the Beiping armored train arrived from Jinan and will go to Sangyuan. The special train arrived in Jinan at 4:50 PM, and I also returned to Jinan with the train. It is heard that Mao Qihuan, the head of the Jinan Traffic Department, telegraphed from Dezhou to Jinan this morning, ordering the seventh and eighth trains from Jinan to Yanzhou to be changed to the ninth and tenth trains between Jinan and Dezhou. However, it is impossible to satisfy one without harming the other, and it is not yet known whether it can be realized. As for the issue of the Tianjin-Jinan through train, because there are currently no vehicles, it must be decided after the Director of the Railway Administration, Sun Hegao, has consulted with the authorities in Tianjin. (28th)

Jiao Railway Employee He Zhusan Arrested

Qingdao correspondence: He Zhusan, a clerk in the Electrical Affairs Section of the Traffic Department of the Jiaoji Railway Bureau, was arrested by the Public Security Bureau at around 11:00 AM on the 25th of this month. The reason for his arrest was suspected of being a reactionary. It is said that He Zhusan's original name was Jiru, and he was from Linyi, Shandong. During the 15th year of the Republic of China [1926], he served under Zhang Zongchang, specializing in investigating the activities of the Min Party. In the 16th year, the Central Government secretly sent Zhang Weicun (currently the director of the Shandong Provincial Party Rectification Committee and Training Department) to Lu to work secretly. Zhang led comrades to establish a hospital on Zhengjie Street in Xuzhou as a secret agency of the Kuomintang. Later, the Central Government sent Chuan Siyi, a graduate of the third class of the Whampoa Military Academy, to work on propaganda, living in the hospital established by Zhang. He Zhusan and Zhang Chuan were both from the same hometown and often associated with each other, so He learned about Zhang's secret work and secretly reported it to Zhang Zongchang, who ordered a strict search of the hospital established by Zhang. Fortunately, Zhang Weicun was out at the time and was spared from disaster, but Fu Siyi and Zhang's wife and more than ten members of the propaganda team were arrested and suffered a brutal death. Recently, the Second Propaganda Team of the General Headquarters came to Qingdao to work and learned of this matter. After returning to Jinan, they immediately petitioned the Central Government to order the Shandong Provincial Party Department to arrest He Zhusan and bring him to justice. After being approved by the Central Government, the Shandong Provincial Party Department was ordered to handle it. After receiving the order, the Provincial Party Department sent a letter to the Jiaoji Railway Management Committee, requesting that He be escorted to Jinan for transfer to Beijing. The Jiaoji Railway Bureau immediately replied to the Provincial Party Department, requesting that they directly consult with the administrative or judicial authorities for execution. The Provincial Party Department then secretly telegraphed the Qingdao Municipal Party Affairs Steering Committee to handle the matter on its behalf. The Municipal Steering Committee consulted with the Railway Party Department on a solution and sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau, requesting that it send personnel to arrest He. On the 25th, the Public Security Bureau sent two officers in a car to the General Affairs Office of the Railway Bureau to make contact and take He back to the bureau for detention. In the future, this case may need to be transferred to Jinan for handling. (September 27th)

Rigorous Defense Against Korean Communists in Jilin Province

Admonishing Koreans Not to Cause Trouble in Chinese Territory

Jilin Correspondence: Last month, Korean communist disturbances along the Jidun Railway line in Jilin were quite rampant. Similar incidents have also been frequently discovered in other locations. All captured offenders have been executed by the authorities, and the rest have been dispersed. Recent reports indicate that these communist bandits appear to have fled south to Panshi and Huadian counties. A few days ago, leaflets were discovered near the Yantongshan station on the Ji-Hai Railway. The military and provincial authorities immediately telegraphed orders to the military and civilian officials in the area to strengthen security along the railway line to prevent incidents. Both authorities have also established an anti-communist office to specifically handle anti-communist matters. However, as most of the bandits are Korean, and the province has nearly ten thousand Koreans, managing them is already difficult under normal circumstances. With the rampant communist bandits, suppression becomes even more challenging. Furthermore, the Japanese often overstep their bounds. If not addressed fundamentally, the potential hidden dangers are unimaginable. Therefore, the provincial government has ordered the Civil Affairs Department to draft twenty-two articles for investigating Korean household registrations, submitting them to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee for approval, and ordering all counties and bureaus to thoroughly investigate and report to have grounds for investigation in case of accidents. Simultaneously, both authorities jointly issued a public notice prohibiting red infiltration and wrote an article advising all Korean nationals, stateless individuals, and residents not to propagate communism in China. The article is written in both Chinese and Korean to attract the attention of the Korean people. The following is the text of the advisory to the Korean people: (There is now a kind of evil doctrine similar to pestilence, which spreads the fastest and causes death the fastest. What is it? It is communism. This doctrine is a barbaric egalitarianism. Simply put, it means that those who have no food will eat from those who have food. If anyone tries to implement this doctrine, they will first create two opposing enemies: the people who want to protect their bowls of rice and the government that wants to maintain order. This doctrine is absolutely impossible to implement. Now, some Koreans have been infected by this doctrine and have come to China to implement communism, provoking the Chinese people to unite and resist you, and provoking the Chinese government to resolutely suppress you. You are trying to seize other people's rice bowls to solve your livelihood problems, but before you can get your hands on the rice bowls, you will lose your lives. Isn't this too uneconomical? Moreover, you Koreans and we Chinese were originally one family. Since the Shang and Zhou dynasties, when Jizi was enfeoffed in Joseon, this is a historically verifiable fact. Since you separated from China and became independent, you have become estranged from China. After you merged with Japan, you have become even more estranged from China. However, the Chinese government and the Chinese people still remember the history that we were originally one family and have never treated you unfairly. First, let's talk about the Koreans who have naturalized as Chinese citizens. You have no Korean-organized country, so you naturalize in a Chinese-organized country. Once you have become Chinese citizens, you are Chinese people. The Chinese government allows you to naturalize, which is always a good intention. One is to pity your situation and make you people with a country. The other is to give you protection and hope that you will be very good people. Therefore, the Chinese government has always treated Korean citizens who have naturalized the same as Chinese people, without any discrimination. You should also have some conscience, live peacefully and quietly, so that the Chinese government likes you, and the Chinese people love you. That is the right way. Next, let's talk about the Korean residents in China. After the merger of Japan and Korea, even if you were Koreans in the past, now you are considered Japanese. However, Japan is a civilized country in the world. Since you have become citizens of a civilized country, when you come to reside in our Chinese territory, you should have some civilized behavior and add some glory to Japan. Moreover, China and Japan are the most friendly. Therefore, the Chinese government and the Chinese people treat you Korean residents very friendly. If you do things that disturb the peace in China, I am afraid it will hinder the friendship between China and Japan and their people. If the governments and people of China and Japan unite to treat you, then Japan will not recognize you as citizens, and China will not recognize you as friends, and you will suffer. As for the stateless Koreans, they are refugees who sneak into the undeveloped areas of China to reclaim land and live. There are quite a few of these people in the northeastern border of China. According to international law, stateless people are neither protected by international law nor protected by domestic law and should be expelled from the country. If we allow you to stay, it is an act of virtue by the Chinese government. The ancients said that repaying virtue with virtue is the right principle. If you secretly live in other people's territory, secretly reclaim other people's wasteland, secretly enjoy the treatment of other people's citizens, and then arbitrarily cause trouble and harm people, then you will provoke other people to treat you with harsh means. Therefore, Koreans in Chinese territory should not be superstitious about any doctrine or act arbitrarily. As for communism, Koreans cannot implement it in China. If the property of the Chinese people is to be divided equally, each of the 400 million Chinese people can get a share. Koreans are afraid they will not get a share. Even if the idea of ​​fraternity is the basis of communism, the Chinese people are willing to teach foreigners to share their property equally, so that they are no longer poor. But to say that the property of the Chinese people should be divided among foreigners, I am afraid it will be a bit impossible. Please think carefully about it, Koreans. A doctrine must have a purpose to be a good doctrine. If the purpose of Koreans embracing communism in China is to alleviate poverty, it cannot be achieved, then this doctrine should be discarded. Moreover, when this doctrine is implemented, it is necessary to shed blood and fight desperately. After shedding blood and fighting desperately to implement this doctrine that cannot achieve its purpose, this person is either a fool or a madman. If he is a fool, he is an ignorant and foolish person. The Chinese government cannot bear to kill foolish people without teaching them, so we earnestly advise you. If you understand that communism has hundreds of harms and no benefits, quickly repent and live well with the good Koreans. If you do not repent and arbitrarily cause trouble, not only will the Chinese government not tolerate you, but the Chinese people will also unite and treat you like poisonous scorpions and beasts and thoroughly deal with you. Koreans, do not be delusional! Wake up quickly! If you are infected with this evil doctrine of pestilence, there will be no way out!) (September 23)

Cheng Zhenjun Concurrently Serves as Director of the Zhejiang Civil Affairs Department

Cheng Zhenjun, Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Committee and Director of the Construction Department, assumed the concurrent position of Acting Director of the Civil Affairs Department at 9:00 AM today (the 1st) at the Provincial Government. At 10:20 AM, he convened a meeting of all staff members of the Civil Affairs Department to give instructions, and announced the appointment of Wang Huai as Secretary, Wu Daolong as Assistant in the Secretary's Office for drafting documents, Huang Renhao, Secretary, transferred to serve as Section Chief of the Third Section, Gao Bingtai, the original Section Chief of the Third Section, as Inspector, Lü Xiao Liang as Section Chief of the Second Section, Inspector Zheng Yu concurrently acting as Section Chief of the Seventh Section. Dai Shixi, the original Section Chief of the Sixth Section, has been appointed by the Provincial Government as the Magistrate of Wukang County, and the vacancy has been filled by the promotion of Clerk Ren Yijun.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

The County Government Convened a Meeting of District Chiefs: The County Government convened a meeting of district chiefs yesterday to discuss matters such as expanding the county's police brigade and compiling a register of defense donations. It was decided to complete the organization of defense groups under each district within two weeks. These groups are now being reorganized in accordance with provincial orders to strengthen their capabilities. Regulations have been promulgated and are being implemented accordingly. It was decided that each district chief, after reorganizing according to the regulations issued by the province, should submit a list for reporting. Additionally, a temporary motion was made regarding administrative expenses for each district. It was originally determined that 60% would be allocated starting in September. However, due to the heavy workload in each district, it was requested to maintain the original plan. It was decided to temporarily allocate according to the original budget, and the County Government will notify the Finance Bureau.

Suspects in an Alleged Kidnapping Case Issue a Public Notice: The County Government previously received a secret report alleging that Xu Bolong, Zhang A'gen, and Wu Jinchang, who reside in Hougang, were not engaged in proper occupations and were suspected of involvement in the Sun-Wang kidnapping case. The county magistrate ordered the First Branch Bureau to arrest and send them to Songjiang. After repeated interrogations by Chief Zhu of the Public Security Bureau, they firmly denied the accusations and have been sent to the County Government for review. It is reported that the County Government has ordered the First Branch Bureau to collect evidence and has issued a public notice stating that anyone who has been subjected to threats by Xu and others should report immediately for verification.

A Female Bandit in the Kidnapping of the Yin Child Case Escorted for Interrogation: Yin Yalin, a two-year-old child of Yin Xietai in Jiaodao Bay, was kidnapped. The military and police jointly investigated the case. Detective Yang Shijie captured the female bandit Wu Lu'shi in Shanghai, and the hostage was rescued. The female bandit was escorted to the County Government today for interrogation. The magistrate asked who kidnapped the Yin child. According to her confession, it was her lover, Yao Jinshan, who gathered more than 20 people to kidnap him. They have all fled and disappeared. The magistrate ordered Wang to continue the interrogation.

Suzhou

A Boat on the West Mountain Route Intercepted: A boat owned by Jin Denan, traveling from Xishan to Huzhou, was intercepted by a bandit boat with more than ten bandits at Miaoshang Lianshan around 9:00 AM the day before yesterday. Approximately eight passengers, including Ding Hongsheng, Deng Huihu, Shi A'san, and boat people A'jinniang, Wang A'jin, and Zheng Zhangcai, were robbed, with losses estimated at over 500 yuan. Bandits also robbed Lü Yipei's pig boat. On the 30th, it was transporting sixty-six pigs from Yongmao Pig Company in Jiaxing to Suzhou and was robbed of more than one hundred yuan in foreign currency near Huguan Huanghua Jing. Yesterday (the 1st), the boatman Chang Bajin, transporting pigs from Lücheng, Changzhou, was also robbed when passing through the area. The bandits also burned Chang's body with ropes.

Changshu

Police and Bandits Exchange Fire at the Border of Yu and Cheng: It has recently been reported that bandits have been entrenched in Shizhuang, at the border of Changshu and Jiangyin, and cases of robbery and extortion have occurred repeatedly. The police went to suppress them the day before yesterday, but the bandits were numerous and well-equipped, and they opened fire in resistance. The two sides exchanged fire for an hour. As a result, both sides suffered casualties. The police, outnumbered, went to various places for help. It is now reported that after receiving the report, the Jiangyin Fortress Command sent a battalion of soldiers to suppress them and notified the counties of Changshu and Wuxi to send troops to jointly suppress them to eliminate their traces.

Report on the Investigation of Aiyu Estuary: The Meili District Office, in order to prevent the emergence of bandits, specifically requested the County Government to block Aiyu Estuary. The County Government ordered the Director of the Construction Bureau to conduct an inspection before further discussion. It is now reported that Chen Qiwei, Director of the Construction Bureau, went to the province due to business, and Section Clerk Yao Zhenlong, accompanied by Jin Yiqun of the First District Office and Jin Wenqiu of the Sixth District Office, hired a boat to investigate on the morning of the 29th of last month and returned to the city on the afternoon of the 30th. According to the investigator, the Aiyu Estuary is more than one hundred meters wide, and no one lives within three miles on either side. The nearest markets are in Guli Village or Dongtang City. There are a total of five tributary rivers north to Hupu, Xuliujing, and Gaopu Estuary, and the newly opened river in the south directly reaches Yangcheng Lake. In short, Aiyu Estuary is a necessary passage from the sea to the lake and from the lake to the sea and definitely needs to be blocked. However, there is no proper way to block it. If wooden fences are used to block it, the villagers will definitely rise up in opposition because ships have to go around a long distance. Also, if people are used to guard it, who knows if the bandits cannot use weapons to force them to open it or destroy it? If earthen dams are built, the project would be huge and the funds would be lacking, making it difficult to achieve results. According to the investigators, it would be best to block each tributary river, then station fifty or sixty land police in the north, and deploy several water patrol boats, so that the head and tail can cooperate with each other. The Construction Bureau has submitted the investigation results to the County Government for review.

Wuxi

Prisoners Attempting to Escape Sentenced to Additional Imprisonment: Zhu Jinsheng, Zhang A'yi, Shen Yunqing, and Cai Heyuan, four prisoners in the First and Second Cells of the Wuxi County Prison, used small knives and clock knives at 12:00 AM on the night of the 20th of last month to secretly dig a tunnel under the wooden bunk in the Second Cell, intending to escape. Chen Shenggu and other prisoners in the same cell reported to the prison guard, who reported to Chief Guard Wang Weizheng. Chief Wang reported to Prison Official Xia, who surrounded each prisoner one by one. Afterwards, County Magistrate Pan interrogated the four prisoners and confirmed the facts, adding shackles for confinement. Except for Zhu Jinsheng, who had committed a crime in Changzhou and had been sent for by the Changzhou County Government the day before yesterday to be escorted back for trial, Zhou, the hearing officer, questioned Zhang A'yi, Shen Yunqing, Cai Heyuan, and the other four prisoners in court yesterday afternoon. Zhu and the other four prisoners were sentenced in court to one year of imprisonment each for their attempt to escape. After the sentences were pronounced, they were returned to prison. The Wuxi Chamber of Commerce's Views on the Implementation of Business Tax: The Jiangsu Provincial Government has decided to convene representatives of chambers of commerce from various counties on October 1 to discuss the implementation of business tax. After receiving the order, the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce immediately sought the opinions of various industries on the matter. The meeting was held yesterday, and in addition to recommending Cheng Jingtang, the Standing Committee member of the Chamber of Commerce, to attend the meeting in the province, it also cited the speech made by Finance Director Chen when he came to Wuxi to deliver a speech at the Seventh Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society held in Wuxi, saying that the Suzhou Provincial Tax Bureau had organized a preparatory committee attached to the Finance Department with nine members, held three meetings, and had specific measures. It was originally scheduled to implement the tax on October 1. Unfortunately, the war in the north broke out again this year, and the issue of tax reduction was once again thwarted. In terms of the situation, it may not be possible to implement it as scheduled. Moreover, the Ministry of Finance convened a tax reduction committee meeting in 1928, and the most important premise for the general outline of the measures for collecting business tax in various provinces was: (1) Article 8 of Kangwen, the collection of business tax must be carried out after the implementation of tax reduction; (2) Article 7 of the original text, after the implementation of business tax, all existing tooth tax, pawn tax, slaughter tax, etc., in various provinces, as well as other taxes similar to business tax, shall be separately merged or abolished. Based on the above points, before the implementation of tax reduction, local governments resumed classifying and adding special tax bureaus, and the tax collection methods have not been improved. If business tax is implemented again, it will be difficult for merchants to bear. Yesterday, the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce also telegraphed representatives of chambers of commerce in various counties, requesting them to immediately report to the authorities that business tax should be implemented after the implementation of tax reduction in order to alleviate the difficulties of merchants and relieve the people's strength.

A Robbery Attempted Near Furong Mountain: More than twenty bandits with torches and weapons suddenly came to the Yu family in Qianjia Lane on the south side of Furong Mountain in Tianxia City in the middle of the night the day before yesterday. They smashed open the gate with stones and were about to enter the house to search for valuables when the owner held a gun and screamed for help. Hearing the sound, the neighbors also fired their guns in response. The bandits were shocked and fled in a hurry.

Preparing to Establish a Military Training Class: Chen Buyun, commander of the First Garrison Regiment stationed in Wuxi, came to Wuxi from Beijing a few days ago to inspect the local defense. In order to train troops and select military talents, he specifically negotiated with Jin Deyi, the regiment adjutant, to prepare to establish a military training class. Eight corporals from each company will be selected for intensive training. In the future, they will be promoted to the position of squad leader. The training location has been decided to be in the Huishan Ancestral Hall, and Chen Chaolin, the camp adjutant of the Third Battalion, has been appointed as the director to actively handle the matter.

Jiangyin

Banditry in the Western Town Has Been Suppressed: The bandit disaster in the western town has been quelled after the police team and the Fortress Special Service Company went to the countryside the night before last to suppress them. The bandits in Qianzhou Huangcun have retreated, and the missing bugler Lai Desheng and Cao Jitang of the Ligang Group and the Public Security Section have also returned home one after another. Only one farmer in Huangcun Street died, and several policemen were injured. The troops are still searching the countryside and will not be difficult to pacify.

More Wounded Soldiers Continue to Arrive for Rest: Director Wu of the 25th Rear Hospital received a telegram from the Military Medical Department of the General Headquarters the day before yesterday stating that more than 400 wounded soldiers were coming to Cheng for recuperation. Director Wu notified the Public Security Bureau yesterday (30th) to prepare everything. The telegraphs were active all night, and the wounded soldiers came from the Yangtze River and were expected to arrive at the port on the morning of the 1st.

Difficulty Borrowing Due to Barren Land and Poor People: Finance Bureau Director Shen Lunxu received a telegram from the Provincial Education Fund Management Office the day before yesterday requesting a loan of 40,000 yuan. Yesterday, Director Shen telegraphed, pleading for exemption from the loan because Jiangyin was suffering from banditry, barren land, and poor people.

Zhenjiang

Representatives of Chambers of Commerce from Various Counties Come to the Province for a Meeting: The Jiangsu Provincial Government previously intended to implement business tax to compensate for the loss of tax reduction and specifically scheduled September 1 to convene representatives of chambers of commerce from various counties throughout the province to come to the province for a meeting to discuss implementation measures. Later, it was considered that the time was too urgent, so the date was changed to October 1 and telegraphed to the county governments to order the chambers of commerce in various counties to recommend representatives to report to the province in advance. As of last night, 38 chambers of commerce from various counties had arrived with a total of 44 representatives. They gathered at the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce to hold a discussion meeting to exchange views. Most of them advocated implementing the business tax after tax reduction in accordance with the general outline of the tax reduction meeting of five provinces. Change of County Police Captain: Ma Qingfeng, the police captain of Zhenjiang County, was replaced by Fang Ruzhou due to ineffective bandit suppression and was appointed to take over. Fang was ordered to report to the police. However, after receiving the order, Fang believed that the police team in Zhen County was too corrupt and the ammunition was insufficient. At a time when bandits were rampant, he was unwilling to take responsibility for this, so he specifically submitted a resignation to avoid making mistakes. After Hu, the director, received the report, he ordered approval because his resignation was firm and appointed Peng Jian to take over. It is said that Peng, after accepting the appointment, planned to go to work within days.

Yangzhou

General Situation of Educational Funding Difficulties: The difficulty of educational funding in Jiangdu has been going on for more than a day, so that the director has spent his entire time on fundraising and borrowing, with little time to study other things. The difficult situation can already be seen. The educational funding for this year has only been issued until today, which is May of the Gregorian calendar, causing teachers and staff to complain endlessly. The Autumn Festival is approaching, and educational colleagues require that they must be paid for two months to overcome this difficulty. The Education Bureau, in addition to the treasurer promising to pay 10,000 yuan, has no other solutions. According to the number, even if one month is paid, it is still less than 8,800 yuan. As for borrowing, banks and money shops are unwilling to ask about it again due to past credit relations. Therefore, Director Chen of the Education Bureau has been extremely busy these days in this matter. It is not certain whether the teachers and staff who are eagerly looking forward to it will be able to receive one month's payment before the festival.

Election of Directors of the Boy Scouts: At 3:00 PM on the 29th, the County Boy Scout Council held an election meeting at the Party Headquarters. As a result of the election, Du Gongtang, Ye Yangyuan, and Xia Changdi were elected as directors, and Wang Cheng, Wu Dapeng, and Kong Qingsheng were elected as alternate directors.

The Branch Customs Punishes Unmanifested Foreign Goods: The Shenji Wheel Company's Rongfa small tugboat Tonggui, which departed from Zhen and drove on the Zhenqing route, arrived at the Tianfei Palace Bay in the lack of port area of Yangzhou in the evening. After loading the goods, it was docked at the Dongguan passenger loading and unloading area. The customs officers and servants of the Yangzhou and Guan Branch boarded the ship to inspect the goods and found more than 10,000 yuan worth of foreign goods without manifests, which were confiscated. It is said that after mediation, a fine of 4,000 yuan was imposed to settle the matter.

Nantong

The Mutiny of the Bandits in the New Port Town Was Not Successful: At 10:00 PM on the 29th, thirty to forty bandits suddenly arrived in the Xin Gang Town of Langshan West, carrying weapons. They first went to the sentry post of the Public Security Bureau to rob weapons and ammunition, and set fire to the houses in the South City. The merchants rang gongs to alert the police team stationed in Langshan and the Special Industrial Police Team to rush to the scene. The bandits fled and four people were arrested on the spot, along with their weapons, and sent to the County Government. The town did not open for business on the 30th. Self-Help to Relieve the Tidal Disaster: The areas along the river in Tongyi suffered a severe tidal disaster. The County Government reported to the province for relief, but the province ordered that the provincial treasury was currently empty and it was difficult to find a solution. The local government was still required to raise funds for relief.

The Banditry in Yancheng and Funing Has Become Rampant Again: Ma Yuren's troops in Yancheng and Funing areas in northern Jiangsu colluded with local bandits to cause disturbances. The 133rd Brigade went to suppress them, and Ma retreated to Xidang. Recently, a long-distance telephone call from northern Jiangsu stated that 800 to 900 sea bandits of Shen Guanxi's troops had landed in the area, joined forces with Ma, dug trenches and set up cannons in Shanggang and other places, and led the bandits to collect cotton from various salt reclamation companies and harass the situation, which was becoming increasingly unbearable. Li Mingyang went to Hai'an from Rugao on the 30th to concentrate the provincial security regiment's infantry, cavalry, artillery, machine gun detachments, and other teams to suppress them. Although the bandits in Tongtai Jiangbei have been quelled, there are still many ambushes. Li Changjiang, the temporary commander of bandit suppression in the eight counties, telegraphed the county magistrates, saying that the bandits in the counties of northern Jiangsu were rampant and the people were suffering, which was heartbreaking. Previously, the green gauze tents were raised, and the bandits were hiding, hindering the advancement of the suppression. Now, the sorghum has been cut everywhere, and the green gauze tents have passed, so there is nowhere to hide. At this time, the weather is mild, which is a good time to search for and eliminate the remnants of the bandits and annihilate the bandits. It is now limited to two weeks, and the police team, public security bureau, and security regiment of each county must all cheer up and work hard to search and eliminate the bandits, so as to clear the area as soon as possible.

Nanjing

Newly Built Great Compassion Buddha Seven Retreat: The Nanjing Buddhist Lay Buddhist Forest has been established for several months and has built several retreats to superimpose the dead and wounded soldiers from the North and the South to pray for world peace. Now Layman Wang Yiting has initiated the construction of a Great Compassion Buddha Seven Retreat in the forest and invited the abbot of the Shanghai Hai Chao Temple, the old Master Ci Fa, to preside over the seven from September 30. At that time, many permanent residents, good men, and believers in Buddhism will go to burn incense and pray, respectfully recite the Buddha's name, and the Bodhisattva's holy name, and there will be a grand occasion.

Huzhou

Having Eaten Fish and Meat, They Kidnapped His Son: Baique Village, located in the northwest township about nine miles from the city, is located in the mountains and fields, with stone mines and forests. The villagers are mixed, and there are good and bad. In the Dajingwei area of the village, there is Zhang Youxue, a farmer from Henan, who started his career with diligence and thrift and has a little property. On the 25th of this month, Youxue went to the western township to visit relatives, and his eldest son, Lanfu, had not returned to the city. At about 3:00 PM that afternoon, two bandits with Shandong accents and wooden-cased guns suddenly came to his home. Zhang's wife entertained them with tea and cigarettes and provided dinner with fish, meat, and liquor. The bandits were still not satisfied and forced her to kill a chicken. Zhang's wife did not dare to refuse and slaughtered a hen for them. Unexpectedly, after the bandits finished eating, they took out their wooden-cased guns and threatened her not to make a sound. They took away his second son, Changfu, who was seventeen years old. The bandits told Zhang's wife to contact them at a certain place the next day. However, because Youxue had not returned home the next day, she did not contact the bandits. Unexpectedly, the bandits mistakenly thought that the Zhang family intended to ignore them, so at about 6:00 PM on the 26th, they gathered more than twenty people, each carrying guns and weapons, and arrived. Seeing this, the eldest son, Lanfu, fled immediately, but Zhang's wife still prepared dinner. After the bandits finished eating, they asked Zhang's wife for 1,800 yuan in foreign currency. Zhang's wife replied that her husband was not at home and the woman had no power. The bandits instructed her to pay the money at Chenwan, Changxing at noon on the 27th, otherwise there would be unfavorable consequences.

Notorious Bandit Li Zhenghong Arrested at Muqiao: Li Zhenghong, a notorious and fierce bandit, committed crimes such as kidnapping for ransom and robbing delivery tickets in the Yangcun area of ​​Lincheng Bridge, Changxing, and previously plotted to attack Sian, and has been wanted. When the Second Battalion of the Second Regiment of the Security Team stationed in Changxing went to Lincheng Township Muqiao the day before yesterday to suppress the bandits, the bandit Li Zhenghong happened to be there and was captured and brought to the camp. Yesterday, he was escorted by the camp to the headquarters in the city for verification.

<Pinghu P] A Gambler Narrowly Escapes Being Crushed; at a certain tofu shop in the Si Pai Lou area of Zhapu, more than thirty people were enthusiastically playing Pai Gow upstairs yesterday. Suddenly, a loud crash occurred, and the gamblers all fell through the broken floorboards. Chaos erupted. One person nearly died from being crushed and was severely injured. More than ten others suffered injuries to their feet and hands.

[P Xiaoshan

Driven by Economic Hardship, Parents Kill Their Own Daughter: In Sheqian Town, on the border of Shao and Xiao, a farmer named Li Chaosheng, because his family of five was struggling to make a living and could not get enough to eat, suddenly suffered a mental breakdown the day before yesterday (the 28th). He sharpened a kitchen knife and killed his nine-year-old daughter in the middle of the night, inflicting two cuts to the head and one to the heart. Blood flowed profusely, and she died shortly after. The perpetrator has repeatedly attempted to drown himself.

Burglary Followed by Arson: At the home of the Gao family in Xidu, Dangshan Bay, in the eastern district of Xiao County, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived on the night of the 27th. They looted all five bales of cotton and over a hundred silver dollars. Afterwards, they left a fire in the firewood room. As dawn approached, a fire suddenly broke out, reducing two buildings and five flat houses to ashes, resulting in losses of no less than several thousand gold pieces.

Refugees Again Disturb the Peace: Over four hundred refugees speaking with a Hunan accent have arrived in the Jiudun area of Guali, demanding silver and rice from door to door, acting quite fiercely. Yesterday, they again caused trouble in the homes of people in the Shenglin Yifeng area. The Anchang and Guali Public Security Sub-bureaus, fearing that bandits might be mixed in with the refugees, specially dispatched police to collect silver dollars and escort them out of the area to prevent local disturbances.

Bengbu

Recovering Guns and Funds Seized from the New Second Brigade: Officers and soldiers of the 3rd Battalion, 8th Regiment of Zhao Qinglian's New 3rd Brigade, were proceeding east from Fengtai when they were robbed of guns and supplies in the Shitoupou area by a local gun association. Afterwards, Brigade Commander Zhao telegraphed General Commander Chiang for instructions. It is now known that Chiang has telegraphed Wei Lihuang, the commander of the Anhui Northern Garrison, and Zhang Lisheng, the commander of the 2nd Cavalry Division, ordering them to investigate the matter strictly and ensure that the local gun association returns the guns and funds in full. Representatives from Fengtai have already arrived in Bengbu, willing to return the brigade's lost guns and funds. A peaceful resolution is expected soon.

Local News

Fan De-Wen Lectures at Jiaotong University Yesterday

The Three Principles of the People and Socialism

Only Slightly Different in Implementation

Mr. and Mrs. Fan De-Wen, the former Prime Minister of Belgium and leader of the Second International, were warmly welcomed upon their arrival in Shanghai. Yesterday afternoon at four o'clock, Mr. Fan gave a public lecture at Jiaotong University in Xujiahui. Attendees included Cai Yuanpei and hundreds of the university's students and faculty. The topic of the lecture was the Three Principles of the People and Socialism. President Li Zhaohuan delivered an introductory speech. The meeting adjourned around seven o'clock. The text of Mr. Fan's speech is as follows:

Li Zhaohuan's Introductory Remarks: Li Zhaohuan, the President of Jiaotong University, began with an introduction, stating, "It is an exceptional honor to have the world-renowned Mr. Fan De-Wen here today to deliver a lecture. The relationship between China and Belgium has always been extremely friendly. Regarding the Railway Department directly under our university, the engineering work for the Longhai Railway was entirely undertaken by Belgian engineers. Recently, the Belgian government returned the Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity for educational and construction purposes. Furthermore, Mr. Fan is dedicated to promoting world peace, and the Chinese nation is known for its love of peace. With shared ideals and common goals, his presence at our university today is truly an honor in the history of our school."

Thoughts on Visiting the Western Hills: Then Mr. Fan De-Wen stood up and delivered a speech in French, translated by Yang Gongda. He stated, "My visit to China is purely for the purpose of observation and learning. I am definitely not here as a politician to promote any ideology. After arriving in Shanghai, friends have often asked me to discuss various issues, such as my impressions of Soviet Russia, my observations on the Three Principles of the People, and the differences between the Second and Third Internationals. I would like to take this opportunity to humbly offer my personal observations and the perspective of a European to discuss the Three Principles of the People and European Socialism with you. In 1906, Mr. Sun Yat-sen came to Brussels and visited me at the Parliament. I was in a meeting giving a speech, so I had a long conversation with my friends, and at the same time, the Tongmenghui was established in Brussels. This is my direct and indirect relationship with Mr. Sun. During my recent visit to Beijing, I went to the Biyun Temple in the Western Hills. Observing the visitors, I noticed a kind of reverence. It shows that the value of a great man is even greater after his death than during his lifetime. At that time, the efforts of the Kuomintang were not yet widespread, but today, the Three Principles of the People are known to every household."

Discussion of Ideologies: Next, I will discuss the Three Principles of the People from my personal observations. First, regarding Mr. Sun's Principle of Nationalism, there are fundamentally two views in Europe: (1) Aggressive nationalism, which is the use of force to conquer smaller nations. This is absolutely opposed by internationalism and socialism. (2) National self-determination, which is the demand for freedom, independence, and equality by the nation itself. Mr. Sun's Principle of Nationalism belongs to (2). I extremely sympathize with and support it, and I hope it can be realized soon. I especially hope to unite the world's smaller nations to work towards the construction of world justice and truth. Next is the Principle of Democracy. Mr. Sun's principle is based on American President Lincoln's government of the people, by the people, and for the people. Many Europeans believe that China's current level of public intelligence makes it difficult to directly discuss democracy. But I believe this is a necessary process. Therefore, Mr. Sun also said that there should be a transition period from autocracy to democracy, which is the so-called period of political tutelage. During the period of political tutelage, the Nationalist Party guides the gradual development forward, so it is definitely not a regression. I also strongly agree. Next, regarding the Principle of People's Livelihood, in Europe, it is translated as socialism, because the main outline of the Principle of People's Livelihood is similar to socialism in every aspect. The only difference is in the method of implementation. In Europe, because industry is developed and large capitalists are extremely oppressive, socialism advocates that the proletariat unites and strives to achieve its ultimate goal. But Mr. Sun's Principle of People's Livelihood is based on the fact that China is an agricultural country, so it advocates cooperation between labor and capital to resolve disputes. However, due to different environments, the fundamental ideas are no different. Both sides do not argue about this, which I strongly support. Then he spoke about the work of the Second International, saying that the ultimate goal is to seek national equality, freedom, and fraternity."

Slight Change in Itinerary: Mr. Fan was originally scheduled to go to Beijing on the 7th and Hangzhou on the 14th. Now it has been changed to taking the night train to Beijing on the 7th, returning to Shanghai on the night train on the 10th, and going to Hangzhou on the 12th, and returning to Shanghai on the 15th. The Academia Sinica has informed both Beijing and Hangzhou. In addition, the Shanghai World Academy and the Sino-French University have scheduled a tea party to welcome Mr. Fan at 5:00 PM today (the 2nd). It is reported that those invited include Cai Yuanpei, Li Shizeng, Wu Zhihui, Zhang Jingjiang, Wang Jingqi, Zheng Yuxiu, Huang Jinrong, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, and over a hundred others. There will also be a performance of national music by the Datong Music Society.

Ministry of Finance's Opinion on Tax Policy

To be Published Immediately

Statement by Finance Minister Song Ziwen regarding the publication of the Ministry of Finance's Kemmerer Commission's Opinion on Tax Policy: The draft of the Kemmerer Commission of the Ministry of Finance's proposal for China to gradually adopt the gold standard was published in early March of this year. At that time, we intended to publish the commission's other opinions at the same time, but due to the unrest in the current situation, there has been an unexpected delay. It has now been decided to continue publishing the commission's various opinions. In addition to the commission's Opinion on Tax Policy, which will be published immediately, other reports will be disclosed successively in the future.
