Four Organizations Host Banquet for American Professor

To Discuss the International New Calendar System

Mr. Thomson, the former professor of the University of Michigan and the American representative to the 19th International Statistical Conference held in Tokyo recently, and Mr. Coussmuss, the representative of the League of Nations, and Mr. Loomis, the Executive Director of the Pacific Council, have come to China one after another, making a brief stop in Shanghai. The China Critic Weekly, the Chinese Economic Society, the Chinese Statistical Society, and the University of Michigan Alumni Association will host a banquet for the three gentlemen at the Datong Restaurant on Nanjing Road this evening (the 2nd), and have also invited Mr. Lei Mai, professor of economics at the University of Michigan, who came to Shanghai recently, to make academic connections. It is expected to be a grand occasion. Mr. Coussmuss advocates for the International New Calendar System, which divides the year into thirteen months, each with twenty-eight days (four weeks), totaling three hundred and sixty-four days. The twenty-ninth day of the thirteenth month is a public holiday (i.e., New Year's Day), which is more convenient than the twelve-month calendar system. His visit to China is to discuss the issue of dispatching representatives to the International Calendar Reform Conference next year. A small Chinese explanatory booklet has been printed for distribution to various sectors for public discussion.

Record of the Second Day of the National Anti-Drug Week

Grand Opening Ceremony

Today is Anti-Drug Law Abiding Day

The 7th National Anti-Drug Movement Week opened yesterday, and all parts of the country responded uniformly. Various circles actively participated in yesterday's opening ceremony. Many telegrams of congratulations were sent from various places, and reports of events held were numerous. Today is the second day of Anti-Drug Week, namely Anti-Drug Law Abiding Day. The details are recorded as follows:

Opening Ceremony: Yesterday at 2:00 PM, the opening ceremony of the 7th National Anti-Drug Movement Week was held at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. (A) Agenda: (1) Reading the Premier's will; (2) Reading the Premier's anti-drug instructions; (3) Chairman announcing the reasons for the meeting; (4) Reporting on the preparations for Anti-Drug Movement Week; (5) Speeches; (6) Proposals; (7) All taking the anti-drug oath; (8) Closing. (B) Participating groups included Shanghai Municipal Government, Bureau of Health, Bureau of Social Affairs, Bureau of Public Works, Bureau of Public Safety, Shanghai Special District Local Court, Taxpaying Chinese Association, Shanghai YWCA, Chinese Four Abstinence Society, Shanghai Puyi Society, Shanghai Customs Superintendent, Shanghai Medical Association, and over forty other group representatives, as well as Wang Jingqi, Wang Xiaolai, Huang Jiaohui, Shen Chuanyang, Zhou Chucai, and Fu Dingmo, totaling over seventy people, chaired by Wang Jingqi and recorded by Shen Chuanyang. (C) Chairman Wang Jingqi announced the reasons for the meeting, stating that the significance of Anti-Drug Week is to awaken compatriots to rise up against drugs. The drug scourge in our country is becoming increasingly severe, and without a quick remedy, destruction is inevitable. This year's Anti-Drug Week aims to make the people of the country pay attention to the spirit of abiding by the law, understand the importance of implementing anti-drug education, and eliminate domestic opium and restrict the source of foreign opium drugs, which cannot be delayed. (D) Huang Jiaohui, the executive director, reported on the preparations, stating that Anti-Drug Week originated seven years ago. At that time, the people of the country, amidst silence, responded to the call of the association, creating today's great anti-drug movement. There are over four hundred anti-drug groups nationwide. Although there is talk of banning opium, there are still incidents of collecting taxes and extorting donations in various places. The anti-drug movement, although facing difficulties and obstacles, continues to fight as always. The preparations for this year's Anti-Drug Week were more enthusiastic than last year. Events are being held simultaneously in various places today. Our food is scarce, famine is frequent, and the high value of gold and the low value of silver are all caused by the opium drug scourge. After the Anti-Drug Week, it is hoped that compatriots across the country will join together and fight together to achieve the goal of elimination.

Passed Proposals: (1) Requesting the government to abolish the special tax in Hunan and Hubei, resolved (A) that the conference shall formally request the Central Party Headquarters to order the National Government to abolish the special tax in Hunan and Hubei to maintain the ban on opium and preserve the country's reputation; (B) that the conference shall formally write to the Ministry of Finance to abolish the special tax in Hunan and Hubei as soon as possible; (C) that the conference shall formally request the people of Wuhan to jointly urge the implementation. (2) Strictly prohibit the planting of poppies, resolved (A) to telegraph the central government in the name of the conference, instructing the Ministry of Military Affairs to promptly stop the troops stationed in various provinces from forcing farmers to plant opium and collecting opium taxes, and to severely punish the military commanders who collect opium taxes; (B) to telegraph the Central Anti-Opium Commission and the Ministry of Internal Affairs separately, instructing all provinces to notify the county magistrates to conduct thorough surveys of opium seedlings and remove them; (C) to telegraph various opium-producing provinces and regions separately, urging them to jointly resist the acts of taxing and forcing planting; (D) that the anti-drug associations should hold the above-mentioned items every autumn when opium is planted. (3) Conduct a nationwide survey of the opium scourge, resolved that the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association should formulate a survey plan, engage experts, conduct a nationwide survey, and request the central and local governments and various sectors to assist in achieving the goal. (D) Urge the convening of the Second National Anti-Opium Conference, resolved to formally request the National Government in the name of the conference to order the convening in accordance with the promulgated regulations for the organization of the National Anti-Opium Conference, and at the same time to telegraph various organizations across the country to respond to the association's proposals. (E) Compile anti-drug textbooks and request the Ministry of Education to order all levels of schools across the country to adopt them. (F) Request the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association to pay attention to popular anti-drug propaganda for laborers. (G) Request the anti-drug association to request the Ministry of Internal Affairs to order all municipal governments across the country to instruct the social affairs bureaus to investigate the citizens within their jurisdictions and list the number of opium addicts, and report them monthly for comparison, and severely punish local officials for increases and commend and reward them for decreases, and order all provincial and county governments across the country to earnestly prohibit the planting, transportation, smoking, and selling of opium, and investigate and punish those who treat it as a mere formality or dismiss them and never employ them again.

Measures for Law-Abiding Day: (A) Significance: The anti-opium laws in our country are undeniably strict. If they can be earnestly enforced, eliminating the opium scourge will be easy. However, the government authorities have always been constrained in handling opium cases. When encountering influential people, they often hesitate to act, allowing the state officials to set fires while forbidding the common people to light lamps, so that the law is equivalent to being a dead letter and the ban is no different from a mere formality. Every time I think of this, I feel pain. The implementation of the opium ban relies on the law as a vanguard. The eradication of the drug scourge cannot be achieved without rigorously enforcing the law. (B) Purpose: The purpose of Anti-Drug Law Abiding Day is to awaken compatriots to monitor the government, urge officials to strictly ban opium, use fearless spirit to report illegal officials, merchants, and local traffickers, demand the government to investigate public officials smoking opium and severely punish them according to the law as a warning to others, and then promote the education of legal common sense, so that people have the ability to distinguish right from wrong, know what to take and what to reject, know what to oppose and what to follow, and can each fulfill their civic responsibilities, abide by the law automatically, act as a backing for the law, so that corrupt officials and local bullies have no way to reverse right and wrong, confuse black and white, and the eradication of the drug scourge is likely to be achieved. (C) Measures: (1) Widely disseminate anti-opium laws to make the public understand; (2) Petition the local government to earnestly implement anti-opium laws; (3) Collect evidence to report illegal anti-opium officials and merchants and local bullies who privately traffic and plant; (4) Hold a large anti-drug oath.

Outline of Propaganda for Law-Abiding Day: The calamity of opium in China originated from the behavior of imperialists who disregarded international public law and humanitarianism, sacrificing the nations and countries of others to seek their own self-interest. Looking at the introduction of opium, they have deprived our country of countless money and forced us to sign unequal treaties. These people use these unequal treaties to transport opium and drugs into the country to satisfy their desire to poison China, harm others, and benefit themselves. In addition, they publicly sell opium in the areas where overseas Chinese live in the Nanyang Islands, while setting strict laws to protect white people, with those who are addicted being sentenced to ten years in prison. However, this kind of law is ineffective for Chinese people. From this, it can be seen that imperialists, both inside and outside our country, use the law at any time and any place to kill our compatriots and despise our sovereignty. At the same time, they confuse black and white and reverse right and wrong at the League of Nations General Assembly, even saying that our country's opium ban is lax, in order to deceive people. Shouldn't all Chinese people pay attention to this? This is also clear evidence of people despising public law. As for the spread of opium within the country, it is even more clearly contrary to the law. The warlords of various provinces, under the pretext of raising funds, have greatly relaxed the ban, widely collecting taxes, forcing the planting of opium seedlings, and sheltering transportation, and various illegal acts are countless. Since the completion of the Northern Expedition, the National Government has adopted a policy of complete prohibition and ordered the entire country to comply. However, while many have earnestly implemented the policy, there are also quite a few who have set up special agencies to monopolize the opium and collect opium taxes. The bans cannot be consistent, and the people have no target to follow, and the local cases that have occurred repeatedly have not been investigated and punished according to the law. This gives us great suspicion. The Jiang'an local case was ended confusedly, and the large officials transporting opium were not brought to justice. This is what our association does not understand most. Isn't this despising the dignity of the law and destroying the national ban? The ability of opium itself to destroy the law is as described above, and the various evils produced by opium are联带随时随地可发现 We want to eliminate drug scourge today, we should promote the common sense of tobacco prohibition laws, so that the social people have some understanding of the government's prohibition, do not destroy the standards of law, have the ability to identify right and wrong, know where to take and where to reject, can each implement the responsibility of citizens, for the backing of the law. After promoting the education of legal knowledge, we should further promote the people's automatic compliance with the law. Although there are some illegal officials and members of the society with evil forces who despise the law, destroy the tobacco ban, bribery is rampant, and shame is swept away, thus creating an illegal environment. Those who are determined, in view of the deterioration of the situation, mostly hold a negative and pessimistic view. This attitude is not entirely appropriate. We must not be discouraged because of this, but promote the movement of people's automatic compliance with the law in society. Although officials have those who know the law and violate the law, and evil forces are rampant for a while, our pure people have the right to correct them, so that corrupt officials and local bullies are ashamed and have no foothold. From a small number of people to a majority, we can eventually create a great force, so that those who destroy the law and violate the law will move in the right direction. Our country's tobacco prohibition laws are strict and complete. If they can be earnestly implemented to eradicate the tobacco scourge, it will be very easy. However, the government authorities are constrained in handling tobacco cases. When encountering influential people, they often hesitate to act, so that the law is equivalent to being a dead letter, that is, it can only be implemented on ordinary people without power, and there is still no way to interfere with high-ranking officials, wealthy merchants, and what a pity! In the future, the people should bear the responsibility of citizens, implement the monitoring of the government, urge officials to prohibit tobacco in accordance with the law, and must also set an example, and those who violate the law and destroy the law will be abandoned by the people. This move should be especially paid attention to by local people's groups in order to realize the hope of eliminating opium and drugs. All our compatriots should take this as their own responsibility, and the future of the tobacco ban will be successful. Opium is the root of unequal treaties, and unequal treaties have become the talisman of opium. The two evils complement each other, so that our country's affairs are getting worse day by day. Today, foreign opium anesthetic drugs are continuously imported. Our country is restricted by foreign extraterritoriality and cannot crack down on it. Foreign firms and foreigners in various concessions are engaged in public tobacco sales. Our country is also restricted by consular jurisdiction and cannot stop it. The trade of opium is actually dependent on unequal treaties, so unless we find a way to abolish unequal treaties and give our country full sovereignty, our country's opium problem may not be resolved. Otherwise, even if domestic opium is banned, Indian and Persian opium will still be imported in large quantities, and there will be morphine, heroin, cocaine, and other anesthetic drugs produced in various countries to trample on our country's laws and make the harm even worse than before. It is not a blessing for the people, so I hope that comrades who care about the opium problem should pay attention to this point. In short, our country's people's livelihood is poor today, and all kinds of pain are really given by the opium drug scourge. To save the country and save the times, we must strive to restore the movement of tobacco prohibition laws. May the people of the whole country unite during this anti-drug movement week to destroy this opium drug that destroys the law.

Letter to Encourage Manufacturers to Actively Participate

Gao Shuo Urges to Inquire About the San De Tang

Please Reply Immediately to the Jinliyuan Pier Case

The dispute over the Jinliyuan Pier case of the China Merchants Bureau, Gao Shuo, the arbitrator of the bureau, has repeatedly negotiated with the French side. San De Tang has agreed to renew the lease or transfer it and asked the Archbishop of Paris for instructions, but there has been no reply. It has been delayed for three weeks. Gao Shuo sent another letter yesterday, saying that Mr. Lu Bohong and I visited you in the morning of the first day of this month. Regarding the Jinliyuan pier, you immediately agreed to send a telegram to the general hall in Paris to ask for the price, and notify us immediately after receiving a reply. Now it has been more than three weeks. I am very concerned about whether the former reply has returned. Since the new General Office Li of our bureau took office, he urgently wants to get this reply.

Financial Sector Closed Yesterday

Yesterday was the designated holiday for the Chinese merchant silver firms and banks according to the new regulations for the Autumn Festival. All payments and receipts due were postponed to the next day. However, foreign banks and firms remained open as usual. The sixth will be the lunar calendar's Autumn Festival, and banks will be closed for one day, while silver firms will be open as usual.

Silk Factories' Industry Association News Yesterday

Approximately one hundred factories have ceased operations. The local silk factory industry association is demanding the cancellation of the official weight inspection. If it is not cancelled after the six-month trial period expires on October 1st, a strike will be called. Yesterday was the deadline. One hundred and six silk factories in Shanghai, including Ruilun and Xinchang, must wait until their forward silk contracts with foreign firms are cleared before joining the alliance. The rest have ceased operations since yesterday morning, approximately one hundred factories in total.

The District Division Requests Relief: The fifteen subdivisions of the four districts under the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters report that silk sales in foreign firms are extremely sluggish, the stock of silk is increasing daily, and manufacturers lack capital to operate. Silk factories are announcing shutdowns one after another in both the northern and southern parts of the city, leading to a city-wide shutdown trend. The situation is fraught with danger. If all silk factories shut down, hundreds of thousands of workers will be indirectly and directly unemployed. Once their livelihoods are cut off, they may be lured and led by reactionary elements, which will have a significant impact on social security. Therefore, it is urgent to find ways to provide relief to maintain people's livelihoods. A twenty-second party member congress was convened the day before yesterday to discuss and vote on two proposed solutions: (1) Following the Japanese method, the national bank should accept the silk in stock at a high price as collateral; (2) The government should issue silk industry bonds to provide subsidies. The case has been recorded and submitted to the superior party headquarters for forwarding to the central government, requesting the government to adopt and implement these measures quickly to provide relief.

Wusong Fortress Commander Inspects Forts

Deng Zhenquan, the commander of the Wusong Fortress, accompanied by Chief of Staff Teng Jushou and Adjutant Shen Zitian, inspected the Nan Shitou and Bei Shitou forts, Tan Hai lighthouse, and observation post at 8:00 AM yesterday. In the afternoon, they continued to inspect the Shizi Lin fort and the San Guan Tang gunpowder depot. At 4:00 PM, they returned to the headquarters and convened a meeting with Chief of Staff Teng, Adjutant Shen, Ordnance Chief Li, Quartermaster Chief Zeng, Nan Fort Commander Chen Wenyu, Bei Fort Commander Zhou Qing, Shizi Lin Fort Commander Shi Ze, Garrison Battalion Commander Zhang Wenyi, and all officers above the rank of warrant officer for instruction. The main points were to diligently fulfill their duties, emphasize academic research in their spare time, and issue each person a copy of Zeng Wenzheng Gong's Admonitions to be read and studied at all times as a model, to cultivate useful talents for the party and the nation.

Wusong Garrison Conducts Field Exercises

The entire Second Battalion of the Twenty-Seventh Regiment of the Fourteenth Brigade of the Fifth Division stationed in Wusong, led by Battalion Commander Xiong Kexi, conducted squad combat shooting exercises at the Haibin of Beimen in Baoshan at 8:00 AM yesterday. The scattered target was made of large yellow cloth, resembling an enemy's position. During the shooting, each squad leader commanded, and the whole squad fired simultaneously and individually. Most were able to hit the target, and the soldiers were energetic and showed courage when advancing. After the exercise, Battalion Commander Xiong gave a critique to the troops and encouraged them to continue to strive for progress. He then ordered them to return to their original defenses.

The Japanese Consulate Has Submitted for Discussion

The municipal government is raising short-term customs duty bonds to offset rent. The collection has already begun separately in the northern and southern parts of the city. However, there are many foreign residents in Zhabei, and the matter is the same for everyone, so discrimination is not appropriate. Yesterday, Xu Zhi, director of the Municipal Finance Bureau's North City Additional Revenue Office, sent a letter to the Japanese Consul and others explaining this, asking them to instruct all foreign residents to comply. Japanese Consul Iguchi has already submitted the matter to the Japanese Consulate for discussion.

Chu Minyi's Invention of Tai Chi Pushing Hands Device

Won the Highest Award in Belgium

Mr. Chu Minyi, a member of the Central Committee, is a sports expert in our country. In recent years, he has invented scientific Tai Chi pushing hands equipment such as the Tai Chi ball and Tai Chi stick. He has repeatedly performed publicly in China, which has been deeply praised by sports experts and martial arts masters at home and abroad. They all believe it to be a great tool for exercise. Mr. Chu does not want to keep it secret and intends to offer it to the world, so that mankind's path to health can have another shortcut. Therefore, he took advantage of this trip to Belgium to participate in the International Exposition and brought various Tai Chi pushing hands equipment to display in the Chinese Pavilion, with Mr. Jin Shoufeng performing. Thousands of visitors each day praised it endlessly. The Exposition's Awarding Committee also paid close attention to this type of soft martial arts equipment, and some even personally tried it out, all agreeing that it was beneficial and harmless to the body, so they specially awarded it the highest award to show their appreciation for the craftsman.

Representatives of the Citywide Labor Union's Petition Returned to Shanghai Yesterday Morning

The city's entire labor union previously sent five groups of seven representatives to Beijing to petition. As the central government's reply is still pending, they returned to Shanghai yesterday morning to await the response. However, it is reported that the result will be satisfactory.

Foreign Merchant Ships' Chinese Seamen Demand Pay Raises

Shipping Companies Have Not Yet Responded

The Labor Union Issues Further Statements

Hua Dong News Agency reports that the China Seamen's Industrial and Labor Union General Federation submitted demands for pay raises for seamen to Jardine Matheson, Butterfield & Swire, and other foreign shipping companies. They sent letters to the companies on the 29th of last month, setting a three-day deadline for a response. Yesterday was the last day of the deadline, but the employers have not yet responded. Here are the latest news from both labor and management sides:

Labor's attitude: According to Labor Union Secretary Liu Yuzhou, the pay raise requests only apply to the chief stewards, stokers, and deckhands on the North China, South China, and Yangtze River shipping lines of six companies: Jardine Matheson, Butterfield & Swire, Nisshin, Osaka, Asiatic Petroleum, and Mobil, totaling approximately 4,000 seamen. Among them, Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire employ the most seamen. Therefore, if Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire agree to the proposed pay raise conditions, the other four companies will have no problem. If the employers still ignore them today (i.e., today), they will take the second step: warning each branch of the company. If there is still no result, the seamen from the three foreign shipping lines will go on strike to awaken the employers.

Employer's attitude: Jardine Matheson only translated the Chinese letter into English yesterday after receiving it from the labor union, while Butterfield & Swire translated it the day before yesterday and submitted it to the company managers. They must wait for the companies to hold a meeting before deciding on a response. A response may be sent to the labor union today, and the outcome may be satisfactory.

Ri Ri News Agency reports that Jardine Matheson already understands that the foreign seamen's demands are based on the standards of Chinese ships and are not excessive. Furthermore, Butterfield & Swire seems willing to negotiate. The other companies, such as Nisshin and Osaka, are even less of a problem. Therefore, they have changed their approach and their attitude is gradually becoming more moderate. The union has informed the workers not to be too hasty and to wait for negotiations. The seamen also do not want to go to extremes and have agreed to wait another day. If there is still no satisfactory response by tonight (the 2nd), they will send representatives to issue a final warning. If there is still no result, they will go on strike. The preparations for the strike include: (1) striving for unity between new members (waiters, servants, etc.) and old members (sailors, stokers, chief stewards, cargo handlers, etc.); (2) requesting subsidies from the central government to alleviate the economic hardship during the strike. However, according to the person in charge of the Seamen's Industrial and Labor Union, both sides are expected to get closer after negotiations begin.

Wusong Rice Industry Labor Dispute Resolved Yesterday

Three Agreements Signed

All rice industry workers in Wusong Town, in order to urge the employers to fulfill the conditions stipulated by the labor union, petitioned the Eighth District Party Headquarters to convene a meeting. Because the employers did not send representatives to attend, the workers believed that they were deliberately delaying the matter. All employees left their shops on the day before yesterday (September 30). Details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that the matter was mediated yesterday by representatives of the Shanghai Rice Industry Labor Union, together with Yin Gongtian and others from the Eighth District Party Headquarters Executive Committee. As a result of the meeting between labor and management, the employers have recognized three terms, and a treaty was signed with the District Party Headquarters as follows: Wusong Rice Industry Labor-Management Agreement: (1) Pay increase: According to the roster, both parties shall agree. (2) The pay increase conditions shall be implemented from September, and the monthly bonus shall be uniformly one yuan. (3) All those who were dismissed or resigned due to this pay raise movement must be reinstated. The pay increase shall be re-negotiated. After the conditions are agreed upon and signed by both parties, all employees immediately returned to work, and a pay raise movement was resolved.

Work of the Agricultural Products Inspection Office

Wheat... Bee colonies... Sugar products

The Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Office was ordered to inspect wheat in order to eliminate the long-standing practice of mixing cement and impurities. Preparations have been underway for four months. In addition to the implementation already in place in Jiangbei, Shanghai also began work yesterday. It is reported that this preparatory work was carried out under the guidance of Mo Dingsen. Mo graduated from the Montpelier National School of Agriculture in France with a degree in agricultural technology. He is currently a professor of crop science at the Central Agricultural College and a wheat technician. He is indeed a wheat expert. This time, in addition to contacting wheat merchants and flour merchants as much as possible, all the proposed regulations, purchase of instruments, and other work were assisted by Technician Mo. The Ministry of Agriculture originally planned to invite Mo to serve as the director of the second section of the inspection office, but Mo declined because he was already a professor at the Agricultural College and did not want to work in both Beijing and Shanghai. However, he agreed to contribute everything in terms of academics. Therefore, the Ministry of Agriculture appointed Cai Wuji, the deputy director of the institute, to serve concurrently as the section chief. A wheat inspection office was set up within the section, and Jiang Hanluo was appointed as the director to be in charge full-time. The recent work of the inspection office, in addition to wheat, also involves the import of foreign honeybees. Because each bee is infected with larvae, putrid odor, and island and Nosema diseases, the inspection method has been decided in consultation with the customs. Feng Huanwen, a beekeeping expert, will be responsible for the inspection. Feng graduated from the beekeeping department of the University of Wisconsin in the United States. The Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce specially sent him to the United States as a commissioner for beekeeping investigation and a director of the beekeeping training class of the Agricultural and Mining Department. He is currently a professor of beekeeping at the Labor University and has extensive experience in inspecting bee diseases. It is also reported that the Shanghai Inspection Office also plans to prepare for the inspection of sugar products due to repeated requests from sugar merchants to determine the quality and avoid being secretly cheated. Zhou Dayaou has been appointed by the Ministry of Agriculture as the preparator. He holds a master's degree in sugar engineering from Lu Province University in the United States and has practiced in three sugar factories in the United States for many years. He was formerly the manufacturing section chief of the refining sugar factory of the National Sugar Manufacturing Company. He is currently also the vice-chairman of the Executive Committee of the International Society of Sugar Cane Technologists. He has been sent to prepare for this and has already arrived at the office.

Measures to Improve Substandard Wheat After Inspection

Wheat Sorting Yard Set Up in Fuxin Warehouse, Xiaoshadu

The Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Office recently submitted a request to implement the inspection of wheat transported to and sold in Shanghai from October 1 due to the problem of mixing wheat with cement and impurities from time to time. The newspapers have repeatedly reported on this. It is now known that according to the regulations for inspecting wheat, wheat that fails the inspection must be ordered to be improved before it can be sold. The procedure for improving the quality is quite complicated. For example, if the moisture content is too high, there must be a large threshing floor for threshing. If there are too many impurities, windlasses, cages, etc. must be used to remove them. Except for some wheat merchants in Shanghai who have the above equipment and can improve it themselves, the rest, such as wheat merchants and vendors, will definitely feel it difficult and unable to sell. In order to actively improve agricultural products, consider the commercial situation, and seek to facilitate merchants in finding ways to improve, the Wheat Sorting Yard has been set up to facilitate the implementation of various improvement procedures. It is reported that it has been agreed with Fuxin Flour Company to borrow the Xiaoshadu Transportation Warehouse of the company as the Wheat Sorting Yard. There is a large open space there, which is very suitable for spreading wheat, and the equipment such as windlasses and cages is complete and can be used. Wang Yaochen, the manager of the company, is very supportive and willing to cooperate with the Agricultural Inspection Office to achieve the goal of improving agricultural products. Yesterday, the office officially informed the Shanghai and Hanshan Grain Guilds to inform all wheat merchants. The wheat merchants and vendors were all grateful to hear this, believing that this move would benefit all parties.

Yang Zigong Reports on the Tragic Flood in Suizhong

The China Relief Society has received reports from various parties on the tragic flood in Liaoning. Yang Zigong, chairman of the Charity Association of the Four Provinces of Jilin, Rehe, Heilongjiang, and Fengtian, came to Shanghai and reported that in Suizhong County alone, a total of 62,972 people were affected by the disaster, 750 people died in a few days, 28,660 houses were washed away, and 186,612.9 mu of farmland were destroyed. The severity of the disaster is unprecedented. The fields are destroyed and cannot be cultivated, the dead have filled the ravines, and the living are starving to death. Chairman Yang witnessed it with his own eyes and could not bear to speak. The disaster in Suizhong County is like this, and the rest are probably similar. Although the association has telegraphed Tianjin to ask Director She to report on the situation in Suizhong County, where Xikamenwai Avenue was submerged by the flood,

Gui Sheng set up porridge kitchens in Dazhuang and Xiaozhuang, which were the most severely affected by the disaster. In addition to the 10,000 yuan that the association had previously remitted to Suizhong for disaster relief, it remitted another 30,000 yuan from the Shanghai Bank of Communications yesterday for the porridge kitchens to purchase grain. However, the disaster is great and the relief funds are meager. It is impossible to solve the urgent need with a drop in the bucket. The fields are destroyed and cannot be cultivated, and the dead cannot be saved. Without a large sum of money, it will not be enough to relieve the suffering. Chairman Yang brought many photos of the tragic disaster in the county and sent them to the newspapers, hoping that benevolent people at home and abroad would see the tragedy and contribute to saving the catastrophe. Chairman Yang also said that there was a rumor that General Zhu Ziqiao, a great philanthropist in the Northeast, had encountered danger. He and Zhu Zi were returning together from Shaanxi, where they were providing disaster relief. There is no truth to it. It is because others were kidnapped in the places where General Zhu passed by, and passers-by spread the rumor in error. I received a telegram from Liaoning a few days ago that General Zhu will return to Ping from Liaoning soon to carry out disaster relief work.

Inspection Report of the Central Bank

Sixty-Seventh Time

The Central Bank's Sixty-Seventh Inspection Report on Issuance Reserves states: In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this committee is responsible for inspecting the Central Bank's strict exchange coupon reserve. The sixty-seventh inspection was held at the bank's Issuance Bureau on September 30, 1919, and the results of the inspection are announced as follows: Total amount of exchange coupons issued: 19,460,912 silver dollars, including: 18,490,262 silver dollar coupons, 970,650 yuan in subsidiary coin coupons. Total amount of exchange coupon reserve: 19,460,912 yuan, including: 17,022,512 yuan in cash reserve. The cash reserve is calculated as: 12,664,213.27 yuan stored in the bank's issuance treasury, 1,170,867 yuan stored in branches in various ports, and 3,187,431.73 yuan stored in the same industry. Guarantee reserve converted into 2,438,400 silver dollars. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Exchange Coupon Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. September 30, 1919, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Li Fuxun, Supervisors Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiding.

Request for Instructions on Handling Shadow Companies

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted to the Bureau of Social Affairs yesterday: The forwarding, customs declaration industry reports that there are shadow companies using registration and licensing as a means of resistance. What method should be used to provide relief? According to the situation, please submit the matter for review and instruction. On September 26, the Shanghai Forwarding and Customs Declaration Industry Association sent a letter stating that the establishment of the industry association is nothing more than to consolidate the group and protect the industry. However, there is no clear provision on how to resolve the issue of shadow companies' trade names, and there is nothing to defend against. Therefore, a special request for interpretation is made for compliance. If there are members who are not the same as the public, engage in the same business, and have the same trade name, if the shadow company alone directly applies to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for registration and obtains a ministerial license as a means of resistance, if the company that has joined the association for many years requests the industry association to find a way to provide relief, what laws and regulations should the association rely on, or submit to the Bureau of Social Affairs for processing, or send a letter to your association to forward to the superior official for review, the enemy will have no way to resolve it. If it is not justified, the association will lose its ability to protect its members, and there will be no value in the association. I have always looked up to your association as the competent authority for commercial groups. For the above questions, please give clear instructions for compliance, and I will be deeply grateful. According to this, the organization of the industry association is originally to safeguard the common interests of the industry and correct the abuses of the business. Now, if there is a shadow company that engages in the same business with the same trade name and rises up to negotiate, it uses registration with the ministry as a means of resistance, so that legitimate businesses cannot be corrected. If it is not remedied, it will truly affect the protection of the industry association. It is reasonable to submit the matter to your bureau for inspection, to give approval, instruction, and compliance, which will be deeply appreciated.

Local News Two

Power Outage in the Central District of the Public Concession Last Night

Total Darkness for About Half an Hour

The Cause Was Damage to the Transformer Substation

The electricity in the central district of the Public Concession, east of Xizang Road, south of Nanjing Road, west of Fuzhou Road, and north of Avenue Edward VII, suddenly went out at 6:42 PM last night. The streetlights on all the roads were also completely dark. The darkness was comparable to the situation in Zhabei the night before. Light was restored at 7:35 PM. The reason for the blackout was that the electrical transformer substation inside the Wing On Company on Nanjing Road was accidentally damaged, causing a power outage in the central district. The streetlights on the Jing'an Temple Road from the Racecourse to the Carder Road intersection were also completely extinguished.

Filial Son Attempts Matricide with a Knife

Fortunately, Old Father Wields a Stick

Mother Barely Escapes Death

Whether Ms. Ma is the Biological Mother

Court Still Needs to Investigate

Hu Aji of the Hongkou Police Station, No. 526, Three-way Crossing, a native of Shaoxing, is over half a century old and has only one son named Fuzhang, now thirty-three years old. He is idle and addicted to smoking and gambling. Having no ability to support himself, he depends entirely on his parents for food and clothing, and is extremely wasteful. Any money he gets is quickly squandered. Aji and his wife, Ms. Ma, have repeatedly admonished him, but his nature is like a beast, treating their teachings like discarded straw sandals. This has left the elderly couple sighing in dismay. Last month, Aji saw his son's clothes were tattered, resembling a beggar from a low-class institution. Moved by paternal instinct, he prepared new clothes for him to wear, hoping to save face. Aji has served in the police station for over thirty years and has many friends, fearing criticism from others. However, Fuzhang did not appreciate his father's concern and repent promptly. He pawned the new clothes and spent the money on opium dens and gambling dens. As a result, within a few days, he was as destitute as ever. His family currently resides at No. 187, Changkang Lane, north of Route Alabaster, Kaifeng Road. The day before yesterday afternoon, Fuzhang, again penniless, returned home from outside, intending to ask for money. He hesitated to enter directly, pacing back and forth in Changkang Lane. Suddenly, Aji returned from his duties at the police station. As soon as he entered the lane, Fuzhang immediately demanded money. Aji, seeing his unfilial son, angrily ignored him. Unable to obtain money and feeling hungry, Fuzhang had no choice but to go to his uncle's house for dinner. He slandered his parents to his uncle and revealed his rebellious intentions. The uncle, fearing that this would truly escalate into a tragic act of unfilial violence, decided to take precautions. He immediately sent his son to inform Aji. Sure enough, after dinner, Fuzhang, carrying a kitchen knife, rushed back to his parents' house, intending to commit matricide. Reaching Changkang Lane, he saw his mother, Ms. Ma, walking out of the house. Fuzhang, who had been hiding in a dark corner, suddenly rushed forward, grabbing and subduing her. In this critical moment, Aji, who had been informed by his nephew, grabbed a door bar and struck Fuzhang's leg with full force. Fuzhang fell to the ground in agony. Aji seized the knife and went outside the lane, calling two Chinese constables, No. 2809 and No. 2667, who took Fuzhang and the knife to the Huishi Police Station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Special District Court, where Judge Wu Tingqi conducted a preliminary hearing. The police station's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated that the case was originally intended to be prosecuted under Article 294, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Code for attempted assault. However, after investigation, the victims were found to be his biological parents. It should be changed to Article 283, attempted harm to direct ascendants, and prosecuted accordingly. He requested that the law be strictly enforced to maintain ethical principles and uphold social order. Subsequently, the victims, Hu Aji and his wife, recounted the unfilial behavior of their rebellious son and also requested severe punishment. When questioned, Fuzhang surprisingly denied that Ms. Ma was his biological mother, claiming she was his father's concubine, a preposterous and extreme falsehood. He only admitted to having an argument at the lane entrance last night, denying any knowledge of the knife. Because the defendant denied that Ms. Ma was his biological mother, which was a crucial point, the court questioned Hu Aji in detail. Aji clarified that Ms. Ma was indeed his wife and Fuzhang was indeed his biological son, and his brother could testify to this. Judge Wu then ordered the defendant to be detained and scheduled a further hearing in seven days to summon witnesses.

Young Woman Dies Suddenly at Eighteen - Suspicious?

Argument with Husband the Night Before

Death Reported the Next Morning

Husband Seems to Be a Suspect

Court Hearing Held Yesterday

Qian Acai, a native of Ningbo, works on a Yangtze River steamer for a certain shipping company. He married Xuan Axiang, who was only eighteen years old. She lived at No. 711, Yangshupu Road. On the 18th of last month, Qian returned to Shanghai with the ship. When he had time to go home, his wife had not yet washed his changed clothes, so the couple had an argument. The next day, Axiang suddenly died. The Huishan Police Station was notified and dispatched detectives to investigate. Finding Qian Acai suspicious, they detained him and sent him to the Special District Court for interrogation. The court opened yesterday morning. The police station charged Qian with murder under Article 282. Then, a witness, Zhang Rengui, was summoned and testified, "The deceased is my niece. Her residence is half a li away from my home. The couple has always been on good terms. At 7 PM on the evening of the tenth, Axiang came to my house and did not mention any argument with her husband. Unexpectedly, I suddenly heard of her death the next afternoon. I believe she was killed by my nephew-in-law, so I reported it to the police station." Zhang Li, a woman who lived in the same house as the deceased, testified that "The defendant and his wife lived downstairs. During dinner on the evening of the 18th, I heard the couple arguing. At 6 AM the next morning, I got up and went downstairs and saw the defendant sleeping near the door and Axiang was sleeping leaning on a table. Afterwards, I went out to buy groceries through the back door. When I returned, Axiang was already dead. But I saw the condition of the body," and so on. When questioned, the defendant confessed, "Because my wife did not wash my changed clothes, we argued on the night of the 18th. I angrily raised my hand and hit her head twice. Shortly after, my wife complained of abdominal pain, so she went to sleep. Then I also went to sleep. At 7 AM the next morning, I woke up and saw that my wife was no longer sleeping on the bed, but leaning on a table outside the room. Because she was in a place where people walk, and I was afraid of obstructing the entrance and exit of other people in the house, I moved the stool she was sitting on. Unexpectedly, my wife immediately fell to the ground without a sound, her eyes slightly open, and she did not respond when I called her. Only her hands were still warm, so I hired a rickshaw to send her to the hospital, but there was no way to save her, and she soon died," and so on. Judge Feng ordered the defendant to be detained and scheduled another hearing.

Dismembered Male Corpse on Avenue Dubail

Entire Body Divided into Six Sections

Can Be Described as Inhumane

Yesterday afternoon at 6 PM, patrolling constables of the French Concession's Baojian Road Police Station, while patrolling the intersection of Avenue Dubail and Rue des Grosliers, discovered two pieces of luggage, including a trunk and a bundle. Inside was a male corpse, divided into six sections. The legs and feet were divided into four sections and placed in the leather trunk. The body and head were divided into two sections and hidden in the bundle, completely naked, without a thread, with blood and flesh blurred, unbearable to witness. The constable was shocked and immediately reported to the police chief, who personally arrived at the scene. It was determined that the corpse was a man around twenty years old, who was killed with a knife. Detectives were dispatched to carry the corpse to the Tongren Auxiliary Yuan Hall for examination.

Reorganization of the Municipal Finance Bureau's Boat Tax Office

Saving Expenses... Rectifying Tax Revenue

Since the Municipal Finance Bureau abolished the boat tax contractors last year and took over the operation, establishing the Municipal Boat Tax Office and the Wusong, Suzhou River, and Chenjiadu branches, as well as the Xiaoshadu, Puzhao River, and Pudong inspection stations, although boat tax revenue has increased, the Boat Tax Office employed many people and had large expenses, which did not significantly benefit the municipal treasury. Now, Finance Bureau Director Tang Naikang, to reduce expenditure and increase income, has submitted a proposal to the municipal government to reform the organization of the Boat Tax Office. The Dongjiadu, Wusong, Suzhou River and other places will all be renamed as the "So-and-So Boat Tax Office." Each office will have a director, two clerks, and tax collectors and inspectors. The number of people will be reduced by one-third compared to before. Each Boat Tax Office will be directly under the Second Section of the Bureau, with two clerks designated to oversee boat tax matters. Two chief inspectors will be established to inspect the collection work of each office and supervise their compliance. It is reported that after the organizational change, the expenses of each Boat Tax Office will be reduced by more than 7,000 yuan per year compared to the original budget. The bureau order has been published yesterday, and the reorganization will be implemented from October 1st.

Municipal Bureau of Public Works Prohibits Loading and Unloading of Goods in Parking Lots

The Municipal Bureau of Public Works, in order to improve traffic and eliminate danger after the completion of the reconstruction of East Gate Road, had set up parking lots on the northern public land at the eastern end of the road, designating places for parking automobiles and rickshaws, marking boundaries with white paint, and installing signs. However, nearby businesses often used the land to place goods. For example, the Yuantai Hengxing Company set up vegetable stalls in the parking lot a few days ago. They were ordered to write down statements, allowing them to move the goods, and the bureau sent a letter to the district office to investigate and deal with it, and ordered the station police to strictly prohibit it.

Statistical Issues in Kidnapping Cases

Social Bureau Replies to Public Security Bureau

One Reason for Discrepancies in Numbers

The Municipal Social Bureau previously received a letter from the Public Security Bureau, asking for a detailed reply regarding the discrepancy between the statistics of kidnapping cases published by the Social Bureau and the figures found by the Public Security Bureau for verification. It is reported that the statistical materials of the Social Bureau are recorded from newspaper reports, and it is feared that there are some cases not reported by newspapers, but there is no other source of information to draw from, so it has to be used as a basis temporarily. In the statistics, the so-called kidnapping cases include those who kidnap people for ransom. If people are kidnapped for ransom after robbery, they are listed separately in the robbery and kidnapping statistics. Although the perpetrators and victims are the same, the nature is different, so to ensure the accuracy of the statistics, this has to be done. This may be one of the reasons why the number of cases in the Bureau is greater than those investigated by the Public Security Bureau. It is now reported that the Bureau has sent a detailed situation of each case and the dates of the newspapers in which they were reported to the Public Security Bureau for reference, and requested to provide this information in the future for mutual verification.

Vehicle Accident Statistics for September

Thirteen Dead

The Da Mei Evening News reports that, according to the statistics of the Vehicle Affairs Office of the Public Concession Police Station, there were a total of 893 reports of vehicle accidents within the Concession in September, with 13 deaths and 356 injuries. Of these, 11 people were killed by automobiles, and only 2 were due to their own negligence. In the first nine months of this year, there were a total of 8,056 vehicle accident cases, with 108 deaths. Last year, the whole year had only 9,691 cases, with 141 deaths. The vehicles involved in the accident cases last month included 729 automobiles, 68 public buses, 115 trams, and 109 bicycles. Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road were the places with the most accidents, followed by Broadway Road. Pedestrians must be especially careful when crossing these roads.

Person Involved in the Li Jiyun Kidnapping Case

Unintentionally Arrest Two Gang Leaders

Little Wuxi and Little Quan Gen

Detectives Zhu Ziqing, Huang Fusen, Li Wenzhao, etc. of the Old Gate Police Station went out on patrol late at night the night before and, at the intersection of Tibet Road and Dazha Road, saw two people wearing raincoats approaching, with their hands in their pockets. When Detectives Zhu, and the others were about to check, the two men took out pistols, intending to resist arrest. The detectives bravely and unanimously arrested the two men, seized two pistols with ten bullets, and took them to the Old Gate Police Station. Under interrogation, one confessed to the name Yu Guimao, originally from Wuxi, and the other confessed to the name Zhu He, from Shanghai. The police chief ordered them to be detained. According to investigations by the detectives, Yu's nickname was Little Wuxi, and Zhu's nickname was Little Quan Gen. They were actually the leaders of the major case in which more than 10,000 yuan of property was stolen from a certain pharmacy at No. 1681, Xinzha Road. After the case occurred, four members of the gang were arrested, and they have been interrogated and convicted. However, the arrest warrants for the ringleaders Little Wuxi and Little Quan Gen were issued by the court, but because their whereabouts were unknown, they could not be arrested. The detectives were commended by the police chief for unintentionally arresting the two gang leaders. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Special District Court and requested an extension of the interrogation. Because the two thieves were involved in a serious case, it was necessary to conduct a more detailed investigation. Judge Zhou Hanting questioned the two thieves about their age and the circumstances of their arrest and ordered them to be detained for fourteen days for further trial.

Cao Ziliang Commits Suicide Due to Poverty

Takes Poison in the Huizhong Hotel

Cao Ziliang, a native of Changshu, used to work as a bookkeeper in the store attached to the China Public School, now renamed China Primary and Secondary School. Later, due to the wage arrears situation in the school, Cao resigned. He was recommended by Zhu Hejun, the principal of the school, to the Zhaoshangju Tunan Ship, and still worked as an accountant. After the military興, Guonan supplied soldiers and Cao lost his job again. Because his family was not wealthy, it was difficult to be idle, and he could not find a job, so he was very depressed. A few days ago, he met his former servant Cao Yunbo on the road. After talking to each other, he learned that Yunbo had become the deputy manager of the Friendship Knitting Company after leaving school. He told Yunbo that he was staying at Room 88 of the Huizhong Hotel on Sanma Road and invited him to visit him on the 28th. The day before yesterday at noon, Yunbo visited with friends. At that time, the door of Ziliang's room was still closed. After knocking for a long time with no response, the hotel staff felt very strange. Later, they forced the door open and found that Ziliang had taken poison and died in bed. They immediately reported to the Old Gate Police Station, who sent detectives to investigate. They found a package of poison and carried the body to the Philion Road morgue. Yesterday morning, they reported to the Special District Court and commissioned Prosecutor Guo to visit the morgue. After examination, Cao Yunbo declared that he was a fellow townsman and former colleague of the deceased. He had no parents above, no wife or children below, and was all alone. This suicide was purely due to his poor circumstances. Out of friendship, he was willing to claim the remains and provide a coffin. Prosecutor Guo then ordered Cao Yunbo to take the body away for burial.

In the future, we should ask the teachers to spare no effort to guide them patiently." The following resolutions were immediately made: (1) A welcome meeting for new members will be held on October 12 at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Auditorium. There should be martial arts performances. Teachers from each field are responsible for selecting excellent members and preparing fully. (2) Performers should wear uniforms, the style of which is determined by the hall. The material should be domestic goods. The colors are divided into two types: all black for teachers and gray top and black bottom for students, to distinguish them. (3) Those who have practiced martial arts for two years must pass an examination, which is scheduled to be implemented at the end of this year. The types of examinations are divided into three categories: Shaolin boxing, knife, and stick; Wudang boxing and sword. Those who pass will be granted junior graduation. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

The Tenants' Association of Lianyi Company on Guangdong Road held its first executive committee meeting yesterday. Chu Shaoji was the chairman. West Lake Museum Seeks Items

Chen Qi, curator of the Hangzhou West Lake Museum, sent a letter to public organizations and celebrities in Shanghai, saying, "History is the record of mankind, and relics are the evidence for those who study history. The purpose of establishing a museum is to collect evidence for researchers to draw on, so that they can learn from past achievements to promote future progress. During the preparation period of the museum, everything is in its infancy. Everything depends on the people from all walks of life to support this cause. I have long admired your study of history and your rich collection. I am sure you will not hesitate to guide me and correct my shortcomings. Therefore, I would like to present the detailed rules for soliciting items and a list of special items for your guidance, or to share your treasures with the public, or to collect them on your behalf, and enthusiastically support them. It is not only the museum's good fortune, but also the good fortune of social education."

Lost Unnamed Girl Waiting to be Claimed

The Municipal Public Security Bureau yesterday sent a lost unnamed girl from the First District, First Precinct. When asked about her name, age, place of origin, and family situation, she could not answer. It was found that the child was about five or six years old, with a long, round face and cropped hair. She was wearing a white, round-flower-striped foreign cloth long robe, white cloth trousers, was barefoot, and wore green, torn satin shoes. She has now been sent to the Xin Pu Yu Tang orphanage to be cared for while awaiting her family to claim her.

Female Corpse in the Riverbank

Yesterday morning, an unidentified female corpse was discovered in the riverbank about one li west of Guanghua University in western Shanghai. The corpse was estimated to be over sixty years old and was dressed in black clothing. It was discovered by local villagers, who immediately reported it to the local bailiff, Zhang Zhiqing, who then reported it to the local court for inspection.

Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education Explains New and Old Organizational Laws for Student Self-Government Associations

The Ministry of Education, based on a report from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education regarding student self-government associations, has inquired whether they should be handled in accordance with the amended organizational plan for people's organizations, or whether those already organized according to the outline of student self-government association organizations can be exempt from reorganization. The Ministry requested a review and interpretation from the Central Executive Committee. The Ministry of Education issued an interpretation stating: "Received and noted. The principles of student organizations and the organizational outline for student self-government associations have both been approved by the 67th Standing Committee of the Central Government and remain in effect. Student self-government associations in various schools that have been organized in accordance with these principles, the outline, and the social organization procedures approved by the 70th Standing Committee of the Central Government, and whose meetings have been approved by the local senior party headquarters and reported to the competent authorities for record, should be recognized as legal and need not be reorganized. However, in the future, any newly organized student self-government associations, in addition to complying with the organizational principles for student organizations and the organizational outline for student self-government associations, should follow the amended organizational plan for people's organizations in their organizational procedures." This is for your information.

Five Ministries and Agencies to Discuss Foreigners Coming to China to Conduct Scientific Research Today

Recently, foreign organizations have been coming to China to conduct scientific research in a continuous stream. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has consulted with the Ministry of Education on three matters for review: (1) Americans York Robson and others going to Xinjiang for scientific research; (2) British nationals Rick Myers and others carrying weapons to Xinjiang to measure and study glaciers and geology; (3) British national Smith and others carrying weapons to Yunnan and Guizhou provinces to study animals. After the Ministry of Education approved the consultations, it invited the relevant agencies, including the Ministries of Interior, Foreign Affairs, and Military Affairs, and the Academia Sinica, to meet at the Ministry of Education today (the 2nd) to discuss the matter.

Entire Faculty of the Department of Botany at National Central University Resigns

| Departmental Affairs and Classes Completely Suspended |

Students Petition the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Party Headquarters

More than ten students from the Departments of Zoology and Botany at the National Central University have reported that all professors in the Department of Botany have resigned one after another, and departmental affairs and classes have been completely suspended. Although the school authorities have tried to retain the professors, the professors insist on resigning because the fundamental problems have not been resolved. The students went to the Ministry of Education to petition the previous day (the 29th). Minister Jiang happened to be attending a memorial week at the National Government, and Secretary Zhou met with them on his behalf. He accepted the request and acknowledged that the school's administration was poor and that the professors resigned as a result. The school authorities should be held responsible. He will forward the matter to Minister Jiang and hopes to find a proper solution in the near future. The students then sent representatives to the Municipal Party Headquarters to petition, and a certain committee member met with them and promised to provide assistance. The reasons for the professors' resignation are listed below: (1) The research funds from the Cultural Foundation and the Rockefeller Foundation to support the department have been arbitrarily misappropriated by the school. (2) The construction of the Biology Building has become a mere formality, is not aesthetically pleasing, and the structure is not solid. The school authorities did not conduct a careful plan in advance, nor did they supervise the construction responsibly. Half of the construction costs of the building were subsidized by the Rockefeller Foundation, which is a matter of national importance, but the school authorities do not consider making amends. (3) There is no formal dean of the College of Science, and it is difficult to handle matters, etc.

Central University Students Urge Provincial and Financial Parties to Allocate Funds

Recent News from the China Cooperative Society Annual Meeting

The second annual meeting of the China Cooperative Society is scheduled to be held in Hangzhou from October 9th to 13th. The meeting is approaching, and the following are excerpts of the latest news:

Additional Proposals: The society has continued to receive proposals from members in recent days: (1) The society should assist the government in formulating cooperative laws and regulations. (2) The society should promote the organization of the China Cooperative Association (above proposals by Wang Zhixin). (3) The society should find ways to standardize cooperative terminology. (4) Determine the society's funding. (5) Raise the society's fund. (6) The society should establish a cooperative business advisory committee (above proposals by Chen Zhongming). (7) The society should establish liaison offices in various locations where members are located. (8) The society should allow cooperatives and mass education institutions to join as members. (9) The society should raise funds to establish a business advisory department to facilitate the purchase and sale of goods by cooperatives in various locations. (10) A cooperative education committee should be established locally to design and organize various cooperative education activities. (11) Amend the society's organizational plan (above proposals by Cheng Junqing). All of the above, together with the previous cases, have been submitted to Sun Hanbing, director of the proposal section, for review.

Change of Opening Time: The opening day of the conference is October 10th. The time was originally scheduled for 10:00 a.m. However, as the day coincides with National Day, various agencies in Hangzhou will hold a grand celebration, and there may be a conflict in time between the two. Therefore, it has been changed to 2:00 p.m.

Visiting the Tide: The conference period coincides with the tide. The society has specifically scheduled a visit to the tide on the 9th to broaden the participants' horizons. The registration period is scheduled for 9:00 a.m. to 9:00 p.m. on October 9th, and 9:00 a.m. to 2:00 p.m. on October 10th. (4) Members' accommodation will be arranged by the greeters upon arrival at the station, and the cost will be borne by the society. In addition to the meals at the scheduled banquets and tours, please prepare your own meal expenses, miscellaneous expenses, tips, etc.

Liu Jingwen to Study in England

Mr. Liu Jingwen, from Dingyuan County, Anhui Province, is a talented student of the Department of Politics at the National Central University and is also skilled in literature. After graduating in 1929, he took up a teaching position in the senior high school department of Xuzhou High School in Jiangsu. This summer, he took the Anhui Provincial Government's overseas study examination, and due to his academic training, he was among the top scorers. He was approved by the provincial government to be sent to the University of London in England to study politics. It is heard that Mr. Liu has purchased a steamship ticket and is scheduled to sail on October 11th. It is also heard that Mr. Liu's friends in Nanjing will host a farewell banquet for Mr. Liu at the Anle Hotel on the Mid-Autumn Festival.

Local News

Jiangsu Education Funds in Deficit, Borrowing

Shanghai County Borrows 20,000 Yuan

The Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office recently reported that the province's education funds are in an unusual deficit, and that the third month of this year has begun. The education funds for July urgently need to be released and cannot be delayed any further. The office has no choice but to borrow educational funds from other sources to supplement the funds. The office telegraphed the Shanghai County government the other day to borrow 20,000 yuan, which will be offset by the educational funds from the county's autumn and winter taxes for this year. The loan must be repaid within four months of collection. The county magistrate is urged to understand the difficulties of educational funds and do his best to borrow the funds locally and remit half of the funds within days to address the urgent need. Director Wang of the Finance Bureau is currently working with the county magistrate to find ways to borrow the funds. The office also sent commissioners Wu and Jiaxu to the county yesterday to discuss all matters.

Recent News from the 65th Boy Scout Troop

The 65th Boy Scout Troop of China, the Commercial Press Workers' Boy Scout Troop in this city, has been in existence for three years since its establishment. Due to the many events of the 6th Workers' Union, there has been much neglect of the Boy Scout side, so there has not been much development. Since the Reorganization Committee of the Union took office in June of this year, it has deeply realized that Boy Scout training is the only way to cultivate young people. Therefore, it entrusted Wang Wenhua, Liu Yucai, Wang Dingchang, Xie Yanbo, etc. to reorganize the troop and absorb as many young members of the publishing house as possible to provide Boy Scout training. Later, the 7th Board of Directors of the Workers' Union was established and also tried its best to support the troop, so the troop's affairs have become more vigorous than before. Since March, in addition to daily morning exercises, curriculum training has been conducted every Wednesday and Saturday evening, and examinations are held every Sunday. The elementary courses have now been completed, and the Special Savings Custody Committee was also established last month and officially implemented group savings. Other groups, such as the rescue team and the signal flag team, have also been trained and are proficient in succession. At present, on the one hand, new members are being registered with the central government, and on the other hand, preparations are being made for the start of the intermediate courses. At the same time, preparations are being made to participate in the National Day Boy Scout Grand Review in this city, so the work is extremely busy.

Chinese Preparatory International Walking Race

Chinese May Join Walking Race Judging Panel

The Chinese walking team won the championship in last year's Shanghai International Competition due to the serious practice of the team members and the enthusiastic service of the staff. This year, the Association has reappointed Mr. Shi Youhui as honorary director and coach and is scheduled to start official practice next week to prepare for winning the championship again. Also, all the judges of the International Walking Race have been Westerners in the past. The Association questioned the matter with the International Association. The International Association replied with deep apologies and said that they had not appointed Chinese judges because they were unaware of any Chinese who were familiar with the rules of walking races. The International Association has specifically requested the Association to introduce judges in advance for this year's competition. The Association is therefore announcing that anyone who is familiar with the rules of walking races and wishes to serve as a judge should register with the Association's office.

North China Games

Changed to be Held in Shenyang

Shenyang Dispatch: The North China Games of this year, had previously been declared by Hao Gengsheng, the executive member of the association, that due to various reasons, it could not be held. Following the precedent of previous years, it was announced that the games would be cancelled. However, Commander Zhang Xueliang, considering that the Far East Games had recently ended in failure and the North China Games could not be held immediately afterwards, felt that this would expose the country's weaknesses too much. He specifically instructed Hao to find a way to prepare for the games in Shenyang and promised to bear all expenses within the association. Hao then began preparations again. The following is a letter from Hao to a certain party, disclosed below:

Yesterday morning, Commander Zhang summoned me for a conversation, saying that he read in the newspaper that the North China Games would not be held this year, and asked if it was true. I said it was true and reported in detail the progress of negotiations with various parties. The commander then said, "The Far East Games recently ended in failure, and the North China Games cannot be held immediately afterwards, which would expose the country's weaknesses too much. I hope you can find a way to prepare for the games in Shenyang," and asked how much money was needed. I said that the North China Games last year spent too much money, and although the lively scene was unprecedented, it should be regarded as accidental and not set as a precedent. If the games are held in Shenyang this year and prepared according to educational principles, approximately ten thousand yuan would be sufficient. The commander also nodded in agreement. Last night, I conveyed this instruction to Zhang Boqin in Tianjin, and a reply telegram has arrived, which reads: "To Mr. Hao Gengsheng of Northeast University, I agree to hold the North China Games in Shenyang. Qin." This is the general course of events. Results of the Japan-Poland Women's Track and Field Competition

Poland Wins Six Events with Excellent Results

Japanese Hitomi Kinue Wins Three First Places

The track and field competition between Japan and Poland was held on the afternoon of the 11th of this month at the newly built stadium in Warsaw, Poland. As a result, Poland achieved excellent results, winning six of the nine events. On the Japanese side, Hitomi Kinue worked hard and won three first places in high jump, long jump, and javelin. In the overall score, Poland won with 54 points, while Japan lost with 36 points. On the day of the competition, ambassadors from various countries were present. The Japanese ambassador hosted a banquet for the athletes at the embassy. At 10 PM that night, they took a train to Berlin, where they will compete with Germany. Woolen Overcoat Fabrics are Scarce and Prices Rise

Thick woolen overcoat fabrics have been heavily stocked by merchant guilds in recent days, and some transactions have also taken place on this street. Therefore, wholesale transactions of whole boxes by the trade association are extremely prosperous. Unfortunately, the arrival of goods is lacking, and the market inventory is insufficient to meet sales, resulting in prices rising sharply. Thick woolen fabrics that previously sold for 5 taels have now reached over 6 taels. Colorful woolen overcoat fabrics that previously sold for around 2 taels now sell for 2 taels and 8 or 9 qian. For example, Yongfeng's Fanghualedeng yarn woolen overcoat fabrics are now sold at a uniform price of 1 tael and 6 shi, which is more than 20% higher than at the end of last year. Silk and Tea: Autumn Cocoons from Jiangsu and Zhejiang are Continuously Shipped to Shanghai

Statistics Reach Over 10,000 Packages

This year, the autumn silkworm farming in various counties and cities of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces has been actively promoted by both government and merchants. The enthusiasm for raising silkworms has been quite high, and the number of silkworm eggs hatched has doubled. Silk cocoon merchants have also been ordering from various counties and cities due to the lack of raw materials. Cocoon businesses have prepared huge amounts of money to collect autumn cocoons, creating a temporary surge in activity. Unexpectedly, just as the silkworm larvae entered the first sleep stage, the weather suddenly changed dramatically. Continuous autumn rains and a sudden drop in temperature caused widespread silkworm diseases, and the cocoon production was generally poor, with low quality. The amount of cocoons collected by silk cocoon merchants has generally been insufficient. According to investigations, although autumn dried cocoons from various counties and cities in Jiangsu and Zhejiang are currently being shipped to Shanghai by both water and land routes, the total number is only over 10,000 packages.

Autumn Dried Cocoons from Wuxi are Shipped to Shanghai Smoothly Every Day

Over 5,000 Packages Arrive Continuously... Cocoons Boats Fill the Suzhou River

This year, autumn cocoons from various cities and villages in Wuxi have suffered from weather damage, resulting in a poor harvest and low quality. Only one-third of the cocoon businesses have opened scales. A total of 85 or 6 companies have opened in the entire county, but the amount of cocoons collected has been very limited. The cocoon businesses have gradually stopped weighing, and the collected autumn cocoons are now dried and transported to Shanghai in rotation. In recent days, over 5,000 packages of autumn dried cocoons from Wuxi have been shipped, mostly by boat. The cocoon boats are full of garbage in the Suzhou River area, and they are generally stored in bank warehouses.

Yesterday, the foreign firm silk market in this port was effectively suspended. Because various manufacturers opposed public measurement and inspection, yesterday was the last day. The authorities still did not show any signs of cancellation. All silk factories in Shanghai followed the resolution of the general meeting and implemented the previous two or three taels of fall. The Russian Assistance Association for Gongxi has not yet officially opened, so there is basically no market to speak of.

The strike was to fight, in which, except for a small number of silk mills, such as Xinchang Ruilun, due to the relationship of undertaking the ocean line of credit silk, they were told to settle clear, and then rejoined, the rest were all temporarily closed, and other Sichuan, Lu and Li and other silk merchants also have a tendency to respond. The foreign silk market has been effectively suspended,

Seafood: Squid Supply Exceeds Demand

New Goods Flood in, Trade Firms Loosen Market Prices

The existing stocks of old goods in various grades of squid have been sold through. However, according to telegrams from the production area, the harvest of new goods this year is quite abundant. Therefore, the source of new goods in recent days has been unusually active. The business of customer guilds is even more deserted. In places such as Sichuan, Hankou, Shantou, and Guangzhou, which are usually very prosperous, there is now very little activity, resulting in an oversupply and a thick bottom. Trade firm market prices have therefore gradually loosened. Yesterday's trade firm prices were: Xiangguan large slices of high-quality squid sold for 43 taels, medium slices for 41 taels, to 40 taels and 0.05 qian, picked squid for 39 taels, oil slices for 37 or 8 taels, cut blanks for 34 or 5 taels, paired squid for 42 taels, Jinshan squid high-quality goods for 40 taels, ordinary for 37 taels and a half. The market situation is very weak. Unless customer sales become strong, there is little prospect of rising prices.
