Free Talk

Thoughts

— Xiong Zhaofeng

Our thoughts and actions are mostly governed by the environment. As a result, many weak-willed young people are buried in the tombs of the environment and cannot escape.

Regardless of the religion, the first step is to believe that outside the world of phenomena, there is another world that cannot be seen but is greater and constantly communicates with people. This concept is the fundamental belief of various religions throughout history and across cultures.

Human history is like a long record of the struggle for survival.

Life has its ups and downs. Only through adversity can one appreciate the sweetness and value of good times. Yuan Jianzhai said, "(Only after being sick do you realize how wonderful health is)," which is based on experience.

Before studying a problem, one should first pay attention to two aspects: (1) the actual problem; (2) the understanding of the problem. Understanding the problem comes from the actual problem and arises because of the actual problem. The practical aspect is fundamental, while the understanding aspect is not. Therefore, the most important thing about every problem is the practical aspect, not the ideal aspect.

(Generously sacrificing one's life) is a common occurrence in real society. But (calmly facing death) can only be done with great wisdom and courage.

Humanity is more valuable than nature, and spirituality is more precious than the body. (Response)

Talking About Two Extraordinary People

— Yu Yangzhou

Confucius did not talk about strange phenomena, physical strength, disorder, or gods. As for what is beyond the six directions, the sages preserved it but did not discuss it. However, the sages only preserved it without discussing it, not rejecting and disbelieving it. I have two extraordinary friends whose words seem shocking to the world, but their deeds are obvious and cannot be faked. Moreover, many scholars and officials in Shanghai know these two people, and they can be verified. They are not like the ancients who could make up stories. I suppose curious people would want to hear about them.

One is Mr. Qi Chunfang from Yuyao. Mr. Qi is the younger brother of Qi Hengfang, a prominent merchant in Shanghai. (Qi's name was no less famous than Yu Qiaqing's today a decade ago.) He possessed assets of over a million. At the age of forty, he suddenly met an extraordinary person who taught him the art of breathing and guiding. He has persevered for seven or eight years without wavering. He can absorb energy and abstain from grains, eating only a few red dates and a spoonful of water each day. He wears the same coarse linen clothing in winter and summer, not distinguishing between cold and heat. Moreover, he has not changed it once in seven or eight years, and it has no accumulated dirt, which is also strange. After learning the Tao, he used most of his assets to help charitable causes, and the rest he divided among his two sons. He then took a small boat and sailed among the green waters, not involving himself in worldly affairs. He only occasionally attends the spring festivals of his clan. Qi Yang, the former governor of Jiangxi Province, is also a relative of Mr. Qi. He said that Mr. Qi looks like he is in his forties, but his spirit is full of energy, and he looks no different from ordinary people. According to Mr. Qi himself, he can already know a little about good and bad fortune, but he does not tell people's fortunes. He also believes that his foundation is still shallow. If he perseveres, he may become a land immortal.

The other is Mr. Yuan Xilian from Baoshan (the younger brother of Mr. Guanlan). He works as a lawyer in Shanghai. Mr. Yuan once received secret mantras from a Zhuang monk, enabling him to drive gods and command ghosts. One day, a certain gentleman was stung by a centipede, experiencing extreme pain and fainting. Hearing that Mr. Yuan could cure it, he went to his door to ask for help. Mr. Yuan closed his eyes and chanted a mantra, summoning the centipede that had made the mistake, and investigated whether it had any previous grievances with the gentleman. Finding that it should not have stung him recklessly, he reprimanded it severely. The centipede immediately threw itself down the steps and died. It is said that if there are previous grievances, it is revenge for past wrongs, and there is no way to intervene. Mr. Guanlan's wife also knows incantations. Many friends and relatives who ask her to treat them also experience miraculous effects. However, she does not easily show them to others. The world is so vast, there is nothing that does not exist.

Talking Before the Wine

— Chen Boying

Last night, I was drinking with Mr. Zhang Shouyi. He said that the first cup tastes slightly bitter, which is the best taste. The second cup is inferior. I thought the person who warmed the wine did not do it properly. Mr. Zhang then said that in ancient times, wine was always drunk cold, never hot. The rites include the custom of washing the wine vessels, but not warming the wine. Sima Xiangru and Wenjun sold wine in Chengdu, only mentioning personally cleaning the vessels. Lady Guo of Tang Dynasty put wine in a deer intestine, tied both ends, and hung it on the beam. When she wanted to drink, she untied it and sucked from it with her mouth. If she wanted to drink, she would drink at any time, which shows that it was drunk cold. Only Bai Juyi's poem says, "Green ants float in newly brewed wine, a small red clay stove warms it. The sky threatens snow tonight, would you like a cup with me?" This may be the beginning of drinking wine hot. I said that today's wine comes in two types: yellow wine, brewed from rice, and white liquor, brewed from sorghum. Yellow wine is mostly drunk hot, while white liquor is drunk cold. Perhaps white liquor existed first, and yellow wine came later, so it was drunk cold. I record this to discuss with those who like to drink and study antiquity.

Wang Shaolou, a Rising Star of Great Talent

— Xu Xiaoting

Wang Shaolou is the brilliant son of Wang Yulou, a famous Peking opera actor in Beijing. He began practicing at a young age and showed extraordinary talent. He had both natural talent and the right approach. In the past, he and Li Wanchun supported the mansion of the Binqing Society for six or seven years and gradually showed his potential. Yulou trained his son very strictly, especially focusing on the critical issue of voice hoarseness, putting in the most effort to monitor Shaolou. As a result, Shaolou's voice recovered in a very short time and transformed into the sweet, round, and clear voice he has today. It can be said that he achieved his wish. His singing is purely in the style of Shu Yan, and his understanding is extremely rich. Moreover, he personally received instruction from Shu Yan, so his subtle nuances naturally closely resemble Shu Yan's style. Comparing his recordings from two years ago at the Victory Records, such as "Catching Cao," "Zhu Lian Zhai," and "Black Basin Case," with Shu Yan's recordings, one can see that he has never deviated from the original, even in the most subtle details. His physical movements and martial arts skills are solid, thanks to his strong foundation established in childhood. As for his elegant appearance and leisurely demeanor, he is truly a born talent. Moreover, he is at the prime of his youth and strength, and he does not have any bad habits like smoking or drinking to hinder his progress. With such a favorable environment, it is no wonder that he will make a splash. After leaving the Binqing Society this spring, he has frequently performed with Xue Yanqin in Beijing and Tianjin, and his reputation is rising like the morning sun. Many established male opera singers have been overshadowed by him and have become黯然失色 (dispirited). Cheng Yanqiu recognizes his ability and has invited him to perform together. The audience often praises their collaboration as mutually enhancing. She has never treated him lightly because he is new. As a result, Shaolou's name is well-known. I went to Beijing this spring and watched him perform various plays with famous actors such as Yanqiu, Delin, Shouchen, Miaoxiang, and Ruian. Shaolou was able to maintain the dignity of the leading role and win frequent applause. For a young man in his twenties to receive such special treatment, Shaolou has reason to be proud. This time, he is performing at the Shanghai Grand Theater. In addition to popular civil and military plays such as "Scolding Cao," "Catching Cao," "Battle of Taiping," and "Celebrating the Pearl," he will also perform Yu School's "Zhu Lian Zhai," "Dingjun Mountain," "Fa Chang Huan Zi," and the full version of "Borrowing the East Wind," "Qing Guan Ce," and "White Python Terrace." In particular, his collaborations with Yanqiu in "Fa Men Si," "Visiting Mother," "Zhu Hen Ji," "Scolding the Palace," "Red Mane Horse," and the full version of "Liu Yingchun" are most likely to attract audiences. People in Shanghai have not heard Shu Yan's singing for a long time. Now that his disciple Wang Shaolou is here, they can feast their ears.

Recognizing the Value of Ziyi Ink Paste

— He Tianjian

Everyone knows the importance of ink paste and seals on calligraphy and painting. However, no matter how wonderful the seal is, if the ink paste is not good, the seal's wonderfulness cannot be shown. Therefore, ink paste is especially important. There have been many ink paste making methods since ancient times. Some use mugwort down, and some use silk cotton, but they are not refined. Then, there are those who use willow catkins and wild down, which are of better quality and more miraculous. Those who use them think that their skills have exhausted all possibilities and cannot be improved upon. But they do not know that there is also a method using lotus root silk, which truly surpasses the past and present. The person who exhaustively studied the principle and created this method is Mr. Xia Ziyi, an ink paste expert in Shanghai. Mr. Xia has been studying this art for over twenty years. In the beginning, he felt that the ink paste available on the market could not fully satisfy him. He accidentally ate lotus root and obtained silk, and it was as if he had an epiphany. So he tried using the silk, and the results were very good. Indeed, methods using mugwort down and the like are not as good. Therefore, he mixed it with refined gold, beautiful split sand, and aged oil that had been stored for decades. Its miraculous features are that it does not consume oil, does not become sticky, does not bleed when stamped, and leaves no residue or stickiness on the stone after use. The carved text can rise up more than a millimeter on the paper, with edges on all four sides, which is exceptionally beautiful. It can be said that the ink paste is a sight to behold. There is also a type of wild down whose wonderfulness can also surpass others, being comparable to lotus root silk. Mr. Xia produces a total of eight types: miraculous, superb, highly refined, superior, excellent, and good. Lotus root silk is the divine product, while wild down is the marvelous product. The reason why he can achieve this level is that Mr. Xia does everything himself, from grinding the sand, splitting the silk, preparing the down, mixing the paste, and blending the oil, without relying on others. Therefore, there are no flaws. Moreover, Mr. Xia does not profit from this, but only makes it available to the world at the urging of friends. A gentleman not only perfects himself but also shares his happiness with others. I have seven or eight types of ink paste, and I always feel that they are insufficient when I use them. After a painting is completed, my mind and spirit are very happy, but if the ink paste is not good, I feel disappointed. After obtaining Mr. Xia's lotus root silk ink paste, even the slightly inferior types are carmine red, round, and lustrous, with a color like red beans, adding a lot of color to my humble paintings. Therefore, I now know that the secrets of heaven and earth are endless, and it is up to us to explore and obtain them.

New Knowledge for the Family

— Edited by Tian Xu Wo Sheng

Invincible Butterfly Cream can eliminate wrinkles on the face, correct the sagging of the lower eyelids, and reduce crow's feet at the corners of the eyes. It is extremely effective. It should be used twice a day, morning and evening. Take a large amount with the middle fingers of both hands and apply it to the forehead first. Place the thumbs under the ear roots to allow the middle fingers to move freely and remove wrinkles on the forehead. Then, close your eyes and take Butterfly Cream with the middle fingers of both hands, applying it from the hollows of the nose down, turning along the lower eyelids, straight up along the corners of the eyes, and then down from the eyebrows towards the hollows of the nose, forming a circular shape. Massage for a long time until it dries naturally, and then women can apply powder, ensuring a very fine and comfortable application. Even if men do not apply powder, they will feel their face is like jade. Performing this massage daily can truly rejuvenate you. Applying it to the face overnight before sleeping can especially absorb nutrients and resist wind and dust. It is especially necessary for travelers. In the past, every time I went out, my face would always develop a brownish tint, especially during the summer in West Lake. This year, I used Butterfly Cream and spent three months as a guest on West Lake, and my complexion remained unchanged. Therefore, my whole family regards Butterfly Cream as a precious gift. (A Guest Returning from West Lake) Xu noted that the above massage method requires patience to persist, and women often dislike closing their eyes and not looking in the mirror. In fact, Butterfly Cream is harmless to the eyes. Just like Invincible Tooth Powder, rubbing it can actually draw out eye discharge from the corners of the eyes, which is very beneficial. I had many silken thread-like things in my eyes in the past, and they were cured because of this. The glasses I wear have also become weaker and weaker, which proves that it is not harmful but beneficial.

(P.S.) Invincible Butterfly Cream, the large size is priced at 7.5 dimes per bottle, and the second size is priced at 5 dimes per bottle. There are separate regulations for wholesale. It is available in department stores everywhere.

The Anti-Communist Movement of Finnish Farmers (3)

— Liu Zeng, sent from Paris

(2) The Results of the Lapua Movement

As more anti-communist organizations were established in various places, the methods for preventing communist activities also improved daily. In the beginning, they only requested that the government limit the freedom of communist parties to publish and meet, so that their propaganda could not be as smooth as before. Then, they announced that the communist party was a party that undermined patriotism and that all members of parliament and city councilors belonging to the communist party should have their right to attend revoked. Finally, they went on to advocate amending the current constitution so that the communist party would never have a foothold in the parliament and city councils. The following is a resolution submitted by the Lapua Movement's representative body to the President of Finland.

"Communist printing presses and newspapers should be immediately shut down.

Communist organizations in any form should be immediately disbanded.

Communist officials and their key members should be immediately arrested.

Legislative elections should be held after the above conditions are implemented and national security is restored."

The leaders of the Lapua Movement further made the following statement.

"To correct the various rumors about the anti-communist movement, we declare the following. In the southern part of Ostrobothnia, we only attacked one thing, which is communism. Outsiders do not understand the truth and mistakenly call it fascism, or think that we want to overthrow the constitution and implement a dictatorship. All of this is wrong. We will do our best to fight for our goals, and we will not allow any obstacles or difficulties to hinder our progress."

The strength that the Lapua Movement gathered in a short period of time was fully demonstrated at the Helsinki conference on July 7 this year. Twelve thousand farmers from all over the country came to participate in this conference. The President of Finland also attended the conference and gave a patriotic speech. The entire cabinet and General Mannerheim, the victor of the Finnish Civil War, also attended together.

A few days before the Helsinki conference, the government convened the parliament to implement the Lapua Movement's proposals through legal means. Several proposals to amend the current constitution were submitted to the parliament. The content was roughly to prevent parties that attempted to change the form of government from joining the legislature and to restrict the freedoms of assembly and publication. At the second meeting, most members of parliament expressed their support for the government's proposals. However, at the third meeting, the parliament decided to postpone the above proposals until after the next election. Therefore, the President of Finland announced the dissolution of the parliament. The next election is scheduled to be held on October 1.

Warmth in the Heart (285)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Emerald Bamboo Sheds Tears, Her Heart Breaks; Red Lotus Fragrance Fades, a Maiden's Soul Departs

The conditions had been settled, making it impossible for Cuiyun to object. However, as soon as she entered the door, various hardships gradually came. The first thing was that Zhang Yiqing's attitude changed greatly. When she lived outside, although he had one-third of the world, those ten days a month seemed to belong to her exclusively. Moreover, Zhang Yiqing cut off his dalliances after first obtaining his new love for several months. Everyone who newly acquires a concubine is like this. He swears to the heavens that he will no longer play around outside. After a year or so, he gradually felt monotonous and wanted to be active outside again. Since Cuiyun moved back, he seemed to treat her like an item. Once the ownership belonged to him, he was relieved. Having obtained Long, he desires Shu again. It was as if he wanted to obtain a beloved antique. Once he had it in his hands, he could put it on a high shelf. In short, he was not afraid of being taken away by others but was developing other ambitions. Therefore, he initially came back a little later, but later he still spent his days and nights in dissipation and was absorbed outside. The second thing was that Zhang Yiqing's wife's situation was also somewhat different from when Cuiyun first moved back. At first, she said that they would call each other sisters, but she never treated her with the etiquette of sisters. She even asked Cuiyun to do many things around the house. Although Cuiyun had been in a brothel for several years, she had also managed household affairs in her family since she was a child. Now that she was someone else's concubine, she was happy to do some household chores. Later, she taught her to pack opium. She did not refuse. Originally, girls from Shanghai brothels all knew how to pack opium. Although she could not smoke it, she liked to play with it the most. She thought, "I don't smoke anyway. It doesn't matter if I pack it for her." But once she started packing, she had to pack it forever. First, she laid off A'Bao, who had been packing opium for her. She said that saving one person would also save a little expense. She also told Cuiyun that A'Bao was unreliable. She had successfully seduced the master and was a source of trouble in the house, so it was best to dismiss her as soon as possible. In fact, A'Bao was originally unhappy here. It was nothing to pack opium during the day, but at night, in the middle of the night, sometimes it would last until dawn. If Zhang Yiqing lived with Cuiyun, and Zhang Yiqing's wife wanted to call Cuiyun to sleep with him, she would be unhappy and would not give her a good face. Sometimes, behind her back, she would tell the servants that Cuiyun was a fox spirit who was bewitching men. Therefore, when Zhang Yiqing's wife came to call Cuiyun, Cuiyun felt embarrassed and left. Only when she had smoked enough opium could she go to sleep. At least it had to be midnight. Zhang Yiqing's wife felt that bringing Cuiyun was for her to use, as if buying firecrackers to be set off by others.

Dance Hall News

Dahe Dance Hall on North Sichuan Road announces: "Our hall recently followed the order to mourn the death of President Tan, suspending music for three days, and took the opportunity to reorganize and renovate. Those who match the number will receive a prize. Those who are the last ones without a dance partner do not need to buy a dance ticket. Therefore, these days, there are many cars and horses, and ladies and gentlemen are like clouds, which is quite a grand occasion."
